Aligning Agents via Planning: A Benchmark for Trajectory-Level Reward Modeling
Authors: Jiaxuan Wang, Yulan Hu, Wenjin Yang, Zheng Pan, Xin Li, Lan-Zhe Guo
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T12:35:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T07:26:22+00:00
Comments: accepted to ACL 2026 main conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In classical Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), Reward Models (RMs) serve as the fundamental signal provider for model alignment. As Large Language Models evolve into agentic systems capable of autonomous tool invocation and complex reasoning, the paradigm of reward modeling faces unprecedented challenges -- most notably, the lack of benchmarks specifically designed to assess RM capabilities within tool-integrated environments. To address this gap, we present Plan-RewardBench, a trajectory-level preference benchmark designed to evaluate how well judges distinguish preferred versus distractor agent trajectories in complex tool-using scenarios. Plan-RewardBench covers four representative task families -- (i) Safety Refusal, (ii) Tool-Irrelevance / Unavailability, (iii) Complex Planning, and (iv) Robust Error Recovery -- comprising validated positive trajectories and confusable hard negatives constructed via multi-model natural rollouts, rule-based perturbations, and minimal-edit LLM perturbations. We benchmark representative RMs (generative, discriminative, and LLM-as-Judge) under a unified pairwise protocol, reporting accuracy trends across varying trajectory lengths and task categories. Furthermore, we provide diagnostic analyses of prevalent failure modes. Our results reveal that all three evaluator families face substantial challenges, with performance degrading sharply on long-horizon trajectories, underscoring the necessity for specialized training in agentic, trajectory-level reward modeling. Ultimately, Plan-RewardBench aims to serve as both a practical evaluation suite and a reusable blueprint for constructing agentic planning preference data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过规划对齐智能体：轨迹级奖励建模基准
在经典的基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中，奖励模型（RM）为模型对齐提供基础信号。随着大语言模型演变为能够自主调用工具和进行复杂推理的智能体系统，奖励建模范式面临前所未有的挑战——最显著的是，缺乏专门设计用于评估工具集成环境中RM能力的基准。为填补这一空白，我们提出Plan-RewardBench，一个轨迹级偏好基准，旨在评估评判者在复杂工具使用场景中区分偏好轨迹与干扰轨迹的能力。Plan-RewardBench涵盖四个代表性任务族——（i）安全拒绝、（ii）工具无关/不可用、（iii）复杂规划、（iv）鲁棒错误恢复——包含经过验证的正向轨迹和通过多模型自然展开、基于规则的扰动以及最小编辑LLM扰动构建的易混淆硬负样本。我们在统一成对协议下对代表性RM（生成式、判别式和LLM作为评判者）进行基准测试，报告不同轨迹长度和任务类别下的准确率趋势。此外，我们提供常见失败模式的诊断分析。结果表明，所有三类评判者均面临重大挑战，在长程轨迹上性能急剧下降，凸显了在智能体轨迹级奖励建模中进行专门训练的必要性。最终，Plan-RewardBench旨在作为实用评估套件和构建智能体规划偏好数据的可复用蓝图。

The method covers four task families—Safety Refusal, Tool-Irrelevance, Complex Planning, and Robust Error Recovery—with validated positive trajectories and hard negatives constructed via multi-model rollouts and perturbations. Experiments on generative, discriminative, and LLM-as-Judge RMs under a unified pairwise protocol show that all evaluator families face substantial challenges, with performance degrading sharply on long-horizon trajectories, highlighting the need for specialized training in agentic reward modeling.

AVA: Attentive VLM Agent for Mastering StarCraft II
Authors: Weiyu Ma, Yuqian Fu, Zecheng Zhang, Bernard Ghanem, Guohao Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2025-03-07T12:54:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T06:27:53+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We introduce AVACraft, a multimodal StarCraft II benchmark supporting both Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) and Vision-Language Model (VLM) paradigms. Unlike SMAC-family environments that rely on abstract state representations and exclude VLMs, AVACraft provides RGB visuals, natural language observations, and structured state information, enabling systematic comparison between training-based and zero-shot methods across 21 scenarios spanning micromanagement, coordination, and strategic planning. We establish comprehensive baselines: six MARL algorithms (IQL, QMIX, QTRAN, VDN, MAPPO, IPPO) with Swin-Transformer backbones trained for 5M steps, and multiple VLMs including proprietary (GPT-4o) and open-source (Qwen3-VL) models. Results reveal complementary strengths-MARL peaks at 19.3% win rate after 5M steps, while VLMs achieve 75-90% zero-shot with human-aligned decisions-exposing trade-offs between training efficiency, performance ceilings, interpretability, and deployment cost. Code: https://github.com/camel-ai/VLM-Play-StarCraft2.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AVA：精通星际争霸II的注意力视觉语言模型智能体
我们提出AVACraft，一个支持多智能体强化学习（MARL）和视觉语言模型（VLM）范式的多模态星际争霸II基准测试。与依赖抽象状态表示且排除VLM的SMAC系列环境不同，AVACraft提供RGB视觉、自然语言观察和结构化状态信息，使得在涵盖微操、协作和战略规划的21个场景中，能够系统比较基于训练的方法与零样本方法。我们建立了全面的基线：六个MARL算法（IQL、QMIX、QTRAN、VDN、MAPPO、IPPO）搭配Swin-Transformer骨干网络，训练500万步；以及多个VLM，包括专有模型（GPT-4o）和开源模型（Qwen3-VL）。结果揭示了互补优势——MARL在500万步后达到19.3%的胜率峰值，而VLM以人类对齐的决策实现75-90%的零样本胜率——暴露了训练效率、性能上限、可解释性和部署成本之间的权衡。代码：https://github.com/camel-ai/VLM-Play-StarCraft2。

Adaptive Action Chunking via Multi-Chunk Q Value Estimation
Authors: Yongjae Shin, Jongseong Chae, Seongmin Kim, Jongeui Park, Youngchul Sung
First: 2026-05-11T06:14:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T06:14:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Action chunking emerged as a pivotal technique in imitation learning, enabling policies to predict cohesive action sequences rather than single actions. Recently, this approach has expanded to reinforcement learning (RL), enhancing behavioral consistency and reducing bootstrapping errors in value function estimation. However, existing methods rely on a fixed chunk length, creating a performance bottleneck as the optimal length varies across states and tasks. In this paper, we propose Adaptive Action CHunking (ACH), a novel offline-to-online RL algorithm that dynamically modulates chunk length during both training and inference. To find the optimal chunk length for a dynamically varying current state, we simultaneously estimate action-values for all candidate chunk lengths in a single forward pass, using a Transformer-based architecture. Our mechanism allows the agent to select the most effective chunk length adaptively based on the current state. Evaluated on 34 challenging tasks, ACH consistently outperforms fixed-length baselines, demonstrating superior generalization and learning efficiency in complex environments.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of fixed action chunk lengths in reinforcement learning, which creates a performance bottleneck as optimal chunk length varies across states and tasks. The authors propose Adaptive Action Chunking (ACH), an offline-to-online RL algorithm that dynamically modulates chunk length during both training and inference. ACH uses a Transformer-based architecture to estimate action-values for all candidate chunk lengths in a single forward pass, enabling the agent to select the most effective chunk length adaptively based on the current state. Evaluated on 34 challenging tasks, ACH consistently outperforms fixed-length baselines, demonstrating superior generalization and learning efficiency in complex environments.
该论文针对强化学习中固定动作块长度造成的性能瓶颈问题，提出了一种自适应动作分块算法（ACH），该算法是一种离线到在线的强化学习方法，能够在训练和推理过程中动态调整块长度。ACH采用基于Transformer的架构，通过单次前向传播同时估计所有候选块长度的动作价值，使智能体能够根据当前状态自适应地选择最有效的块长度。在34个具有挑战性的任务上的评估表明，ACH始终优于固定长度的基线方法，在复杂环境中展现出更强的泛化能力和学习效率。
Generative Adversarial Post-Training Mitigates Reward Hacking in Live Human-AI Music Interaction
Authors: Yusong Wu, Stephen Brade, Aleksandra Teng Ma, Tia-Jane Fowler, Enning Yang, Berker Banar, Aaron Courville, Natasha Jaques, Cheng-Zhi Anna Huang
First: 2025-11-22T02:12:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T05:35:39+00:00
Comments: v3: fix the Figure numbering bugs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most applications of generative AI involve a sequential interaction in which a person inputs a prompt and waits for a response, and where reaction time and adaptivity are not important factors. In contrast, live jamming is a collaborative interaction that requires real-time coordination and adaptation without access to the other player's future moves, while preserving diversity to sustain a creative flow. Reinforcement learning post-training enables effective adaptation through on-policy interaction, yet it often reduces output diversity by exploiting coherence-based rewards. This collapse, known as ``reward hacking'', affects many RL post-training pipelines, but is especially harmful in live jamming, where musical creativity relies on dynamic variation and mutual responsiveness. In this paper, we propose a novel adversarial training method on policy-generated trajectories to mitigate reward hacking in RL post-training for melody-to-chord accompaniment. A co-evolving discriminator separates policy trajectories from the data distribution, while the policy maximizes the discriminator output in addition to coherence rewards to prevent collapse to trivial outputs. We evaluate accompaniment quality and output diversity in simulation with both fixed test melodies and learned melody agents, and we conduct a user study with the model deployed in a real-time interactive system with expert musicians. Quantitative evaluation and user feedback demonstrate improved output diversity, harmonic coherence, adaptation speed and user agency. Our results demonstrate a simple yet effective method to mitigate reward hacking in RL post-training of generative sequence models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：生成对抗后训练减轻人机实时音乐交互中的奖励破解
生成式AI的大多数应用涉及顺序交互，用户输入提示并等待响应，反应时间和适应性并非关键因素。相比之下，实时合奏是一种协作交互，需要实时协调和适应，无法预知对方未来动作，同时保持多样性以维持创作流畅性。强化学习后训练通过在线策略交互实现有效适应，但常因利用基于一致性的奖励而降低输出多样性。这种崩溃称为“奖励破解”，影响许多RL后训练流程，但在实时合奏中尤为有害，因为音乐创造力依赖于动态变化和相互响应。本文提出一种新颖的对抗训练方法，基于策略生成的轨迹来减轻旋律到和弦伴奏的RL后训练中的奖励破解。共同进化的判别器将策略轨迹与数据分布分离，而策略在最大化判别器输出的同时，兼顾一致性奖励，以防止崩溃为平凡输出。我们通过固定测试旋律和学习型旋律智能体在模拟中评估伴奏质量和输出多样性，并在实时交互系统中部署模型，与专业音乐家进行用户研究。定量评估和用户反馈表明，输出多样性、和声一致性、适应速度和用户能动性均有提升。我们的结果展示了一种简单有效的方法，用于减轻生成序列模型RL后训练中的奖励破解。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses reward hacking in reinforcement learning post-training for generative AI, specifically in live human-AI music interaction where output diversity is crucial for creative flow. The authors propose a generative adversarial post-training method where a co-evolving discriminator distinguishes policy-generated trajectories from real data, while the policy maximizes both coherence rewards and discriminator output to prevent collapse to trivial outputs. Evaluated through simulations with fixed melodies and learned agents, as well as a user study with expert musicians in a real-time system, the method demonstrates improved output diversity, harmonic coherence, adaptation speed, and user agency, effectively mitigating reward hacking.
本文针对生成式AI在强化学习后训练中的奖励破解问题，特别是在实时人机音乐交互中输出多样性对创意流畅性至关重要的场景。作者提出了一种生成对抗后训练方法，通过一个共同演化的判别器区分策略生成的轨迹与真实数据，同时策略最大化判别器输出和连贯性奖励，以避免输出坍缩为平凡结果。在固定旋律和智能体模拟以及专家音乐家实时交互系统的用户研究中，该方法展示了更好的输出多样性、和声连贯性、适应速度和用户自主性，有效缓解了奖励破解问题。
Consolidation-Expansion Operator Mechanics:A Unified Framework for Adaptive Learning
Authors: Debashis Guha
First: 2026-05-11T04:19:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T04:19:45+00:00
Comments: 38 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Every adaptive learning system must alternate between two operations: consolidating what it already knows and expanding into new evidence. We propose \emph{Consolidation-Expansion Operator Mechanics} (OpMech), a framework that makes this structure precise. The central object is the \emph{order-gap} $\Ogap(θ; e)$, the degree to which a consolidation operator~$Q$ and an expansion operator~$P_e$ fail to commute at a given knowledge state. Because the order-gap is computable from the system's own trajectory, it serves as a real-time control signal: large values indicate that the system is still sensitive to the ordering of consolidation and expansion; once the order-gap falls and stays small, further processing is unlikely to change the outcome. Three results give the signal precise meaning: the order-gap decays along convergent trajectories; a persistently large order-gap implies the system is far from its settled state; and an order-gap-based stopping rule terminates with provable guarantees in both noiseless and bounded-noise settings. The framework applies across five domains: bandits, reinforcement learning, stochastic optimization, continual learning, and recursive language models. We give conditions under which the order-gap reliably tracks convergence in three representative cases. We develop the recursive language model application in detail, showing how OpMech replaces heuristic stopping rules and fixed recursion budgets with principled, evidence-driven alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巩固-扩展算子机制：自适应学习的统一框架
每个自适应学习系统必须在两种操作之间交替：巩固已有知识并扩展至新证据。我们提出“巩固-扩展算子机制”（OpMech），该框架精确刻画了这一结构。核心对象是“序间隙”$\Ogap(θ; e)$，即巩固算子$Q$与扩展算子$P_e$在给定知识状态下未能交换的程度。由于序间隙可从系统自身轨迹计算得出，它可作为实时控制信号：大值表明系统仍对巩固与扩展的顺序敏感；一旦序间隙下降并保持较小，进一步处理不太可能改变结果。三个结果赋予该信号精确含义：序间隙沿收敛轨迹衰减；持续较大的序间隙意味着系统远离稳定状态；基于序间隙的停止规则在无噪声和有界噪声设置下均具有可证明的保证。该框架适用于五个领域：赌博机、强化学习、随机优化、持续学习和递归语言模型。我们给出了在三个代表性案例中序间隙可靠跟踪收敛的条件。我们详细开发了递归语言模型应用，展示了OpMech如何用基于原则、证据驱动的替代方案取代启发式停止规则和固定递归预算。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Consolidation-Expansion Operator Mechanics (OpMech), a unified framework for adaptive learning that formalizes the alternation between consolidating existing knowledge and expanding into new evidence. The key innovation is the order-gap, a computable metric measuring the degree to which consolidation and expansion operators fail to commute at a given knowledge state, which serves as a real-time control signal for system convergence. The authors prove three theoretical results: the order-gap decays along convergent trajectories, a persistently large order-gap indicates the system is far from settling, and an order-gap-based stopping rule provides provable guarantees in both noiseless and bounded-noise settings. The framework is demonstrated across five domains including bandits, reinforcement learning, stochastic optimization, continual learning, and recursive language models, with detailed application to recursive language models showing that OpMech replaces heuristic stopping rules and fixed recursion budgets with principled, evidence-driven alternatives.
该论文提出了巩固-扩展算子力学（OpMech），这是一个统一的自适应学习框架，形式化了巩固已有知识与扩展新证据之间的交替过程。核心创新是序间隙，这是一个可计算的度量，用于衡量在给定知识状态下巩固算子和扩展算子未能交换的程度，并作为系统收敛的实时控制信号。作者证明了三个理论结果：序间隙沿收敛轨迹衰减；持续较大的序间隙表明系统远离稳定状态；基于序间隙的停止规则在无噪声和有界噪声设置下均提供可证明的保证。该框架在五个领域中得到验证，包括赌博机、强化学习、随机优化、持续学习和递归语言模型，其中对递归语言模型的详细应用表明，OpMech用基于原则、证据驱动的替代方案取代了启发式停止规则和固定递归预算。
Learning Approximate Nash Equilibria in Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via Mean-Field Subsampling
Authors: Emile Anand, Ishani Karmarkar
First: 2026-03-04T06:14:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T04:03:08+00:00
Comments: 57 pages, 10 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many large-scale platforms and networked control systems have a centralized decision maker interacting with a massive population of agents under strict observability constraints. Motivated by such applications, we study a cooperative Markov game with a global agent and $n$ homogeneous local agents in a communication-constrained regime, where the global agent only observes a subset of $k$ local agent states per time step. We propose an alternating learning framework $(\texttt{ALTERNATING-MARL})$, where the global agent performs subsampled mean-field $Q$-learning against a fixed local policy, and local agents update by optimizing in an induced MDP. We prove that these approximate best-response dynamics converge to an $\widetilde{O}(1/\sqrt{k})$-approximate Nash Equilibrium, while separating the sample complexities between the joint state and action spaces. Finally, we validate our results in numerical simulations for multi-robot control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过均值场子采样学习合作多智能体强化学习中的近似纳什均衡
许多大规模平台和网络化控制系统在严格的观测约束下，由一个集中决策者与大量智能体群体交互。受此类应用启发，我们研究了一个通信受限场景下的合作马尔可夫博弈，其中包含一个全局智能体和n个同质局部智能体，全局智能体每时间步仅观测k个局部智能体状态的子集。我们提出了一种交替学习框架(ALTERNATING-MARL)，其中全局智能体针对固定局部策略执行子采样均值场Q学习，而局部智能体通过在诱导MDP中进行优化来更新。我们证明这些近似最佳响应动力学收敛到~O(1/√k)近似纳什均衡，同时将联合状态和动作空间的样本复杂度分离。最后，我们在多机器人控制的数值模拟中验证了结果。

The authors propose an alternating learning framework called ALTERNATING-MARL, in which the global agent performs subsampled mean-field Q-learning against a fixed local policy while local agents optimize their policies in an induced MDP. Theoretically, they prove that this approximate best-response dynamics converges to an Õ(1/√k)-approximate Nash Equilibrium, with sample complexities separated between joint state and action spaces. Numerical simulations on multi-robot control validate the theoretical findings.

HAGE: Harnessing Agentic Memory via RL-Driven Weighted Graph Evolution
Authors: Dongming Jiang, Yi Li, Guanpeng Li, Qiannan Li, Bingzhe Li
First: 2026-05-11T03:41:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:41:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Memory retrieval in agentic large language model (LLM) systems is often treated as a static lookup problem, relying on flat vector search or fixed binary relational graphs. However, fixed graph structures cannot capture the varying strength, confidence, and query-dependent relevance of relationships between events. In this paper, we propose HAGE, a weighted multi-relational memory framework that reconceptualizes retrieval as sequential, query-conditioned traversal over a unified relational memory graph. Memory is organized as relation-specific graph views over shared memory nodes, where each edge is associated with a trainable relation feature vector encoding multiple relational signals. Given a query, an LLM-based classifier identifies the relational intent, and a routing network dynamically modulates the corresponding dimensions of the edge embedding. Traversal scores are computed via a learned combination of semantic similarity and these query-conditioned edge representations. This allows memory traversal to prioritize high-utility relational paths while softly suppressing noisy or weakly relevant connections. Beyond adaptive traversal, HAGE further introduces a reinforcement learning-based training framework that jointly optimizes routing behavior and edge representations using downstream tasks. Finally, empirical results demonstrate improved long-horizon reasoning accuracy and a favorable accuracy-efficiency trade-off compared to state-of-the-art agentic memory systems. Our code is available at https://github.com/FredJiang0324/HAGE_MVPReview.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HAGE：通过强化学习驱动的加权图演化实现智能体记忆
在智能体大语言模型系统中，记忆检索常被当作静态查找问题处理，依赖平面向量搜索或固定的二元关系图。然而，固定图结构无法捕捉事件间关系的变化强度、置信度及查询相关依赖性。本文提出HAGE，一种加权多关系记忆框架，将检索重新定义为在统一关系记忆图上进行序列化、查询条件化的遍历。记忆被组织为共享记忆节点上的关系特定图视图，每条边关联一个可训练的关系特征向量，编码多种关系信号。给定查询后，基于LLM的分类器识别关系意图，路由网络动态调制边嵌入的对应维度。遍历得分通过语义相似度与这些查询条件化边表示的学习组合计算，使记忆遍历能优先选择高效用关系路径，同时柔和抑制噪声或弱相关连接。除自适应遍历外，HAGE进一步引入基于强化学习的训练框架，利用下游任务联合优化路由行为与边表示。最后，实验结果表明，与最先进的智能体记忆系统相比，HAGE在长程推理准确性及准确率-效率权衡方面均有提升。代码见https://github.com/FredJiang0324/HAGE_MVPReview。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes HAGE, a weighted multi-relational memory framework for agentic LLM systems, motivated by the limitations of static memory retrieval methods like flat vector search or fixed binary graphs that fail to capture varying relationship strengths and query-dependent relevance. The method organizes memory as relation-specific graph views over shared nodes, where edges have trainable feature vectors; a query triggers an LLM-based classifier to identify relational intent, and a routing network dynamically modulates edge embeddings to compute traversal scores via a learned combination of semantic similarity and query-conditioned representations, with reinforcement learning jointly optimizing routing and edge representations. Empirical results show that HAGE improves long-horizon reasoning accuracy and achieves a favorable accuracy-efficiency trade-off compared to state-of-the-art agentic memory systems.

Rethinking Expert Trajectory Utilization in LLM Post-training for Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Bowen Ding, Yuhan Chen, Jiayang Lyv, Jiyao Yuan, Qi Zhu, Shuangshuang Tian, Dantong Zhu, Futing Wang, Heyuan Deng, Fei Mi, Lifeng Shang, Tao Lin
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-12-12T11:13:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:19:23+00:00
Comments: ACL-26, Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) dominate the post-training landscape for mathematical reasoning, yet differ fundamentally in their reliance on expert trajectories. To understand the optimal way to harness these trajectories for maximizing performance, we propose the Plasticity-Ceiling Framework. This framework empirically grounds the post-training landscape by decomposing the final performance ceiling into the foundational SFT performance and the subsequent RL plasticity (i.e., the maximum improvement via RL). Through extensive benchmarking, we establish the Sequential SFT-then-RL pipeline as the superior standard, overcoming the stability and premature convergence deficits inherent in synchronized approaches. Furthermore, we derive precise scaling guidelines: (1) Transitioning to RL at the Stable or Mild Overfitting Regime of SFT maximizes the final ceiling by securing a robust SFT foundation with substantial RL plasticity; (2) Refuting the ``Less is More'' hypothesis in SFT-then-RL scaling, we demonstrate that Data Scale determines the primary post-training potential, while Trajectory Difficulty acts as a performance multiplier; and (3) The Minimum Validation Loss of SFT serves as a reliable indicator for selecting the expert trajectories that maximize the ultimate performance ceiling. Our findings provide actionable guidelines for extracting maximum value from expert trajectories.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新思考大语言模型数学推理后训练中的专家轨迹利用
监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）主导了数学推理的后训练领域，但两者在依赖专家轨迹方面存在根本差异。为理解如何最优利用这些轨迹以最大化性能，我们提出了可塑性上限框架。该框架通过将最终性能上限分解为基础SFT性能和后续RL可塑性（即RL带来的最大改进），从经验上奠定了后训练格局的基础。通过广泛基准测试，我们确立了顺序SFT-then-RL流程作为优越标准，克服了同步方法固有的不稳定性和过早收敛缺陷。此外，我们推导出精确的缩放准则：（1）在SFT的稳定或轻度过拟合阶段过渡到RL，通过建立稳健的SFT基础并保留大量RL可塑性，最大化最终上限；（2）驳斥SFT-then-RL缩放中的“少即是多”假设，证明数据规模决定后训练的主要潜力，而轨迹难度作为性能倍增器；（3）SFT的最小验证损失可作为选择最大化最终性能上限的专家轨迹的可靠指标。我们的发现为从专家轨迹中提取最大价值提供了可操作指南。
Summary / 总结
The paper rethinks how expert trajectories are best utilized in post-training large language models for mathematical reasoning, comparing Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL). The authors propose a Plasticity-Ceiling Framework that decomposes the final performance ceiling into SFT foundation and subsequent RL plasticity, and through extensive benchmarking, they establish the Sequential SFT-then-RL pipeline as superior to synchronized approaches. Key experimental results show that transitioning to RL at the Stable or Mild Overfitting Regime of SFT maximizes the final ceiling, refute the 'Less is More' hypothesis by demonstrating that Data Scale determines primary potential while Trajectory Difficulty acts as a multiplier, and identify Minimum Validation Loss of SFT as a reliable indicator for selecting optimal expert trajectories.
该论文重新思考了在大型语言模型数学推理后训练中如何最优利用专家轨迹，比较了监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）。作者提出了可塑性-上限框架，将最终性能上限分解为SFT基础和后续RL可塑性，并通过广泛基准测试确立了顺序SFT-then-RL流程优于同步方法。主要实验结果表明，在SFT的稳定或轻度过拟合阶段过渡到RL能最大化最终上限，驳斥了'少即是多'假设，证明数据规模决定主要潜力而轨迹难度作为性能乘数，并发现SFT的最小验证损失是选择最优专家轨迹的可靠指标。
expo: Exploration-prioritized policy optimization via adaptive kl regulation and gaussian curriculum sampling
Authors: Mingxiong Lin, Zhangquan Gong, Maowen Tang, Qian Li, Chuangchuang Wang, Jian Ma, Sutian Huang, Kai Tang, Haonan Lu
First: 2026-05-11T03:19:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:19:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become the standard paradigm for LLM mathematical reasoning, where Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) serves as the mainstream algorithm. We point out two understudied inefficiencies existing in GRPO. First, the fixed KL penalty coefficient overly restricts policy exploration at stages where the model requires significant deviation from the reference policy. Second, uniform sampling of training questions ignores that moderately difficult problems provide the most informative gradient signals for optimization. We propose Exploration-Prioritized Policy Optimization (EXPO) with two lightweight plug-in modules. The Accuracy-Conditioned KL Scaling (AKL) dynamically adjusts KL regularization strength through a smooth nonlinear function of batch average accuracy, relaxing the penalty when the model underperforms and strengthening it when the model achieves good results. The Gaussian Curriculum Sampling (GCS) assigns sampling weights to questions following a Gaussian distribution centered at moderate accuracy around 0.5, focusing training on the model's learning frontier. We conduct extensive experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B and Qwen3-8B-Base over six mathematical reasoning benchmarks. The results show EXPO steadily surpasses vanilla GRPO. It obtains an absolute gain of 13.34 on AIME 2025 pass@32, rising from 63.33 percent to 76.67 percent, and achieves an average pass@32 improvement of 2.66 on the 8B model. The much larger performance gains on pass@32 compared with pass@1 demonstrate that EXPO effectively enlarges the model's exploration boundary under a fixed inference cost budget.
Verifier-Free RL for LLMs via Intrinsic Gradient-Norm Reward
Authors: Xuexiang Wen, Hang Yu, Linchao Zhu, Gaoang Wang
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-05-11T03:15:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:15:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as a promising post-training paradigm for Large Language Models (LLMs), its dependency on the gold label or domain-specific verifiers limits its scalability to new tasks and domains. In this work, we propose Verifier-free Intrinsic Gradient-Norm Reward (VIGOR), a simple reward that uses only the policy model itself. Given a prompt, VIGOR samples a group of completions and assigns higher within-group rewards to outputs that induce smaller $\ell_2$ norms of the teacher-forced negative log-likelihood gradients under the current parameters. Intuitively, lower gradient norms suggest the completion aligns better with the current policy, serving as an intrinsic preference signal for policy optimization. To make this intrinsic signal practical for RL, we correct the systematic length bias of averaged token-level gradients with a $\sqrt{T}$ scaling, and apply group-wise rank shaping to stabilize reward scales across prompts. Across mathematical reasoning benchmarks, VIGOR outperforms the state-of-the-art Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) baseline, and it also exhibits cross-domain transfer to code benchmarks when trained only on math data. For instance, on Qwen2.5-7B-Base post-trained on MATH, VIGOR improves the average math accuracy by +3.31% and the average code accuracy by +1.91% over this baseline, while exhibiting more stable training dynamics. The code is available at https://github.com/ZJUSCL/VIGOR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于内在梯度范数奖励的无验证器强化学习用于大语言模型
尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）近期已成为大语言模型（LLM）有前景的后训练范式，但其对黄金标签或领域特定验证器的依赖限制了其在新任务和领域上的可扩展性。本文提出无验证器内在梯度范数奖励（VIGOR），一种仅使用策略模型本身的简单奖励。给定提示，VIGOR采样一组补全，并对当前参数下教师强制负对数似然梯度的ℓ2范数较小的输出分配更高的组内奖励。直观上，较低的梯度范数表明补全与当前策略更一致，可作为策略优化的内在偏好信号。为使该内在信号适用于强化学习，我们通过√T缩放校正平均令牌级梯度的系统性长度偏差，并应用组内排名整形以稳定跨提示的奖励尺度。在数学推理基准上，VIGOR优于最先进的内部反馈强化学习（RLIF）基线，且仅在数学数据上训练时即展现出向代码基准的跨域迁移能力。例如，在MATH上后训练的Qwen2.5-7B-Base上，VIGOR相比该基线将平均数学准确率提升3.31%，平均代码准确率提升1.91%，同时展现出更稳定的训练动态。代码见https://github.com/ZJUSCL/VIGOR。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes VIGOR, a verifier-free reinforcement learning method for large language models that uses the intrinsic gradient-norm of the policy model itself as a reward signal, eliminating the need for external verifiers or gold labels. The method samples multiple completions per prompt, assigns higher rewards to those with smaller L2 norms of teacher-forced negative log-likelihood gradients, corrects length bias with a sqrt(T) scaling, and stabilizes rewards via group-wise rank shaping. On mathematical reasoning benchmarks, VIGOR outperforms the RLIF baseline, achieving a +3.31% improvement in math accuracy and a +1.91% improvement in code accuracy when trained only on math data, with more stable training dynamics.
该论文提出了VIGOR方法，一种无需验证器的强化学习方法，利用策略模型自身的内在梯度范数作为奖励信号，从而避免对外部验证器或标签的依赖。该方法对每个提示采样多个输出，将教师强制负对数似然梯度的L2范数较小的输出赋予更高奖励，通过sqrt(T)缩放校正长度偏差，并采用组内排名整形稳定奖励尺度。在数学推理基准上，VIGOR超越了RLIF基线，仅在数学数据上训练后，数学准确率平均提升3.31%，代码准确率平均提升1.91%，且训练动态更加稳定。
Your Language Model is Its Own Critic: Reinforcement Learning with Value Estimation from Actor's Internal States
Authors: Yunho Choi, Jongwon Lim, Woojin Ahn, Minjae Oh, Jeonghoon Shim, Yohan Jo
First: 2026-05-08T10:49:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:09:39+00:00
Comments: Under Review; Project Page: https://elijah0430.github.io/poise/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for Large Reasoning Models hinges on baseline estimation for variance reduction, but existing approaches pay a heavy price: PPO requires a policy-model scale critic, while GRPO needs multiple rollouts per prompt to keep its empirical group mean stable. We introduce Policy Optimization with Internal State Value Estimation), which obtains a baseline at negligible cost by using the policy model's internal signals already computed during the policy forward pass. A lightweight probe predicts the expected verifiable reward from the hidden states of the prompt and generated trajectory, as well as token-entropy statistics, and is trained online alongside the policy. To preserve gradient unbiasedness despite using trajectory-conditioned features, we introduce a cross-rollout construction that predicts each rollout's value from an independent rollout's internal states. Because POISE estimates prompt value using only a single rollout, it enables higher prompt diversity for a fixed compute budget during training. This reduces gradient variance for more stable learning and also eliminates the compute overhead of sampling costs for detecting zero-advantage prompts. On Qwen3-4B and DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B across math reasoning benchmarks, POISE matches DAPO while requiring less compute. Moreover, its value estimator shows similar performance to a separate LLM-scale value model and generalizes to various verifiable tasks. By leveraging the model's own internal representations, POISE enables more stable and efficient policy optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：你的语言模型即是自身的评判者：基于演员内部状态的价值估计进行强化学习
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大规模推理模型中依赖于基线估计来降低方差，但现有方法代价高昂：PPO需要与策略模型规模相当的评论家，而GRPO需要每个提示多次采样以保持经验组均值的稳定。我们提出基于内部状态价值估计的策略优化（POISE），通过利用策略前向传播中已计算的策略模型内部信号，以极低成本获得基线。一个轻量级探针从提示和生成轨迹的隐藏状态以及令牌熵统计量中预测期望的可验证奖励，并与策略在线联合训练。为了在使用轨迹条件特征时保持梯度无偏性，我们引入了一种跨采样构造，即从独立采样的内部状态预测每个采样的价值。由于POISE仅使用单次采样估计提示价值，因此在训练过程中，对于固定的计算预算，它能够实现更高的提示多样性。这降低了梯度方差，使学习更稳定，并消除了检测零优势提示的采样成本计算开销。在Qwen3-4B和DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B上，针对数学推理基准测试，POISE在匹配DAPO性能的同时所需计算量更少。此外，其价值估计器表现出与独立的大语言模型规模价值模型相似的性能，并能泛化到各种可验证任务。通过利用模型自身的内部表示，POISE实现了更稳定、更高效的策略优化。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high computational cost of baseline estimation in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large reasoning models, where methods like PPO require a separate critic model and GRPO needs multiple rollouts. The authors propose POISE, which uses a lightweight probe trained on the policy model's internal hidden states and token-entropy statistics to predict expected rewards, avoiding extra computation. A cross-rollout construction ensures unbiased gradient estimation. Experiments on Qwen3-4B and DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B across math reasoning benchmarks show that POISE matches the performance of DAPO while requiring less compute, and its value estimator generalizes to various verifiable tasks.
该论文针对大型推理模型在基于可验证奖励的强化学习中基线估计计算成本高的问题，指出PPO需要独立的评论家模型而GRPO需要多次采样。作者提出POISE方法，利用策略模型前向传播时已计算的内部隐藏状态和词元熵统计信息，通过轻量级探针预测期望奖励，避免了额外计算。通过跨轨迹构造确保梯度无偏估计。在Qwen3-4B和DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B上的数学推理基准实验中，POISE在计算量更少的情况下达到了与DAPO相当的性能，且其价值估计器能泛化到多种可验证任务。
LEPO: Latent Reasoning Policy Optimization for Large Language Models
Authors: Yuyan Zhou, Jiarui Yu, Hande Dong, Zhezheng Hao, Hong Wang, Jianqing Zhang, Qiang Lin
First: 2026-04-20T07:05:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T03:02:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recently, latent reasoning has been introduced into large language models (LLMs) to leverage rich information within a continuous space. However, without stochastic sampling, these methods inevitably collapse to deterministic inference, failing to discover diverse reasoning paths. To bridge the gap, we inject controllable stochasticity into latent reasoning via Gumbel-Softmax, restoring LLMs' exploratory capacity and enhancing their compatibility with Reinforcement Learning (RL). Building on this, we propose \textbf{\underline{L}}atent R\textbf{\underline{e}}asoning \textbf{\underline{P}}olicy \textbf{\underline{O}}ptimization~(\textbf{LEPO}), a novel framework that applies RL directly to continuous latent representations. Specifically, in rollout stage, LEPO maintains stochasticity to enable diverse trajectory sampling, while in optimization stage, LEPO constructs a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens. Extensive experiments show that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for discrete and latent reasoning.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LEPO, a framework addressing the limitation of deterministic inference in latent reasoning for large language models by injecting controllable stochasticity via Gumbel-Softmax, which restores exploratory capacity and enables compatibility with reinforcement learning. The method applies RL directly to continuous latent representations, maintaining stochasticity during rollout for diverse trajectory sampling and constructing a unified gradient estimation for both latent representations and discrete tokens during optimization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LEPO significantly outperforms existing RL methods for both discrete and latent reasoning tasks.
该论文提出了LEPO框架，针对大型语言模型潜在推理中确定性推理导致无法探索多样化路径的问题，通过Gumbel-Softmax注入可控随机性，恢复模型的探索能力并增强与强化学习的兼容性。该方法将强化学习直接应用于连续潜在表示，在展开阶段保持随机性以采样多样化轨迹，并在优化阶段构建统一的梯度估计，同时优化潜在表示和离散令牌。大量实验表明，LEPO在离散和潜在推理任务上显著优于现有的强化学习方法。
VISD: Enhancing Video Reasoning via Structured Self-Distillation
Authors: Hao Lin, Kunyang Lv, Xu Jiang, Jingqi Tian, Zhongjing Du, Jiayu Ding, Qiaoman Zhang, Hongbo Jin
First: 2026-05-07T12:13:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T02:55:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training VideoLLMs for complex reasoning remains challenging due to sparse sequence level rewards and the lack of fine grained credit assignment over long, temporally grounded reasoning trajectories. While reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) provides reliable supervision, it fails to capture token level contributions, leading to inefficient learning. Conversely, existing self distillation methods offer dense supervision but lack structure and diagnostic specificity, and often interact unstably with reinforcement learning. In this work, we propose VISD, a structured self distillation framework that introduces diagnostically meaningful privileged information for video reasoning. VISD employs a video aware judge model to decompose reasoning quality into multiple dimensions, including answer correctness, logical consistency, and spatio-temporal grounding, and uses this structured feedback to guide a teacher policy for token level supervision. To stably integrate dense supervision with RL, we introduce a direction magnitude decoupling mechanism, where rollout level advantages computed from rewards determine update direction, while structured privileged signals modulate token level update magnitudes. This design enables semantically aligned and fine grained credit assignment, improving both reasoning faithfulness and training efficiency. Additionally, VISD incorporates curriculum scheduling and EMA based teacher stabilization to support robust optimization over long video sequences. Experiments on diverse benchmarks show that VISD consistently outperforms strong baselines, improving answer accuracy and spatio temporal grounding quality. Notably, VISD reaches these gains with nearly 2x faster convergence in optimization steps, highlighting the effectiveness of structured self supervision in improving both performance and sample efficiency for VideoLLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VISD：通过结构化自蒸馏增强视频推理
训练视频大语言模型进行复杂推理仍具挑战性，原因在于稀疏的序列级奖励以及缺乏对长时间、时间性推理轨迹的细粒度信用分配。虽然基于可验证奖励的强化学习提供了可靠的监督，但它无法捕捉词元级贡献，导致学习效率低下。相反，现有的自蒸馏方法提供了密集监督，但缺乏结构和诊断特异性，且常与强化学习产生不稳定交互。本文提出VISD，一种结构化自蒸馏框架，为视频推理引入具有诊断意义的特权信息。VISD采用视频感知评判模型将推理质量分解为多个维度，包括答案正确性、逻辑一致性以及时空基础，并利用这种结构化反馈指导教师策略进行词元级监督。为将密集监督与强化学习稳定整合，我们引入方向-幅度解耦机制，其中由奖励计算的轨迹级优势决定更新方向，而结构化特权信号则调节词元级更新幅度。该设计实现了语义对齐的细粒度信用分配，提升了推理忠实度和训练效率。此外，VISD融入课程调度和基于指数移动平均的教师稳定化策略，以支持长视频序列的鲁棒优化。在多个基准上的实验表明，VISD持续优于强基线，提高了答案准确性和时空基础质量。值得注意的是，VISD在优化步骤上实现了近2倍的收敛加速，凸显了结构化自监督在提升视频大语言模型性能与样本效率方面的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Training VideoLLMs for complex reasoning is challenging due to sparse rewards and lack of fine-grained credit assignment over long trajectories. To address this, the authors propose VISD, a structured self-distillation framework that uses a video-aware judge model to decompose reasoning quality into dimensions like correctness, logical consistency, and spatio-temporal grounding, providing token-level supervision. A direction-magnitude decoupling mechanism integrates this dense supervision with reinforcement learning by using rollout-level advantages for update direction and structured signals for magnitude. Experiments show VISD consistently outperforms baselines in answer accuracy and grounding quality, achieving nearly 2x faster convergence.
训练视频大模型进行复杂推理面临奖励稀疏和长轨迹中细粒度信用分配不足的挑战。为此，作者提出VISD，一种结构化自蒸馏框架，利用视频感知评判模型将推理质量分解为正确性、逻辑一致性和时空定位等多个维度，提供令牌级监督。通过方向-幅度解耦机制，将密集监督与强化学习结合，用轨迹级优势决定更新方向，结构化信号调节更新幅度。实验表明，VISD在答案准确性和时空定位质量上持续优于强基线，并实现近2倍的收敛速度提升。
Injecting Distributional Awareness into MLLMs via Reinforcement Learning for Deep Imbalanced Regression
Authors: Yao Du, Shanshan Song, Xiaomeng Li
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-02T11:49:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T02:53:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) struggle with numerical regression under long-tailed target distributions. Token-level supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and point-wise regression rewards bias learning toward high-density regions, leading to regression-to-the-mean behavior and poor tail performance. We identify the lack of cross-sample relational supervision as a key limitation of existing MLLM training paradigms. To address it, we propose a distribution-aware reinforcement learning framework based on Group Relative Policy Optimization, which introduces batch-level comparison-based supervision via the Concordance Correlation Coefficient-based reward to align predicted and ground-truth distributions in terms of correlation, scale, and mean. The framework is plug-and-play, requiring no architectural modification. Experiments on a unified suite of long-tailed regression benchmarks show consistent improvements over SFT and existing MLLM regression methods, with particularly strong gains in medium- and few-shot regimes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化学习为多模态大语言模型注入分布感知能力以实现深度不平衡回归
多模态大语言模型在长尾目标分布下的数值回归任务中表现不佳。基于令牌的监督微调和逐点回归奖励会使学习偏向高密度区域，导致回归到均值的行为和尾部性能低下。我们指出现有多模态大语言模型训练范式缺乏跨样本关系监督这一关键局限。为解决该问题，我们提出一种基于组相对策略优化的分布感知强化学习框架，通过基于一致性相关系数的奖励引入批次级比较监督，以在相关性、尺度和均值方面对齐预测分布与真实分布。该框架即插即用，无需修改架构。在统一的长尾回归基准测试套件上的实验表明，该方法相较于监督微调和现有MLLM回归方法取得了一致改进，在中样本和少样本场景下尤为显著。
Summary / 总结
Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) struggle with numerical regression under long-tailed target distributions due to token-level supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and point-wise regression rewards that bias learning toward high-density regions, causing regression-to-the-mean and poor tail performance. To address the lack of cross-sample relational supervision, the authors propose a distribution-aware reinforcement learning framework based on Group Relative Policy Optimization, which introduces batch-level comparison-based supervision via a Concordance Correlation Coefficient-based reward to align predicted and ground-truth distributions in terms of correlation, scale, and mean. Experiments on a unified suite of long-tailed regression benchmarks show consistent improvements over SFT and existing MLLM regression methods, with particularly strong gains in medium- and few-shot regimes.
多模态大语言模型在长尾目标分布下的数值回归任务中表现不佳，原因是基于token的监督微调和逐点回归奖励会导致模型偏向高密度区域，产生回归到均值的现象并降低尾部性能。为了解决缺乏跨样本关系监督的问题，作者提出了一种基于组相对策略优化的分布感知强化学习框架，通过引入基于一致性相关系数的奖励进行批次级比较监督，使预测分布与真实分布在相关性、尺度和均值上对齐。在统一的长尾回归基准测试集上的实验表明，该方法相比监督微调和现有MLLM回归方法取得了一致改进，尤其在中等样本和少样本场景下提升显著。
Separate First, Fuse Later: Mitigating Cross-Modal Interference in Audio-Visual LLMs Reasoning with Modality-Specific Chain-of-Thought
Authors: Xuanchen Li, Yuheng Lu, Chenrui Cui, Tianrui Wang, Zikang Huang, Yu Jiang, Long Zhou, Longbiao Wang, Jianwu Dang
First: 2026-05-11T02:50:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T02:50:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Audio and vision provide complementary evidence for audio-visual question answering, yet current audio-visual large language models may suffer from cross-modal interference: information from one modality misguides the interpretation of another, thereby inducing hallucinations. We attribute this issue to uncontrolled cross-modal interactions during intermediate reasoning. To mitigate this, we propose Separate First, Fuse Later (SFFL), an audio-visual reasoning framework designed to reduce cross-modal interference. SFFL enforces modality-specific chain-of-thought reasoning, producing separate audio and visual reasoning traces and integrating evidence for answering. We construct modality-preference labels via a data pipeline under different modality input settings. We use these labels as an auxiliary reward in reinforcement learning to encourage a instance-dependent preference for modality cues when answering. We further introduce a modality-specific reasoning mechanism that preserves modality isolation during the separated reasoning stage while enabling full access to cross-modal information at the evidence fusion stage. Experiments demonstrate consistent improvements in both accuracy and robustness, yielding an average relative gain of 5.16\% on general AVQA benchmarks and 11.17\% on a cross-modal hallucination benchmark.
中文标题/摘要
标题：先分离后融合：通过模态特定思维链减轻音视频大语言模型推理中的跨模态干扰
音频和视觉为音视频问答提供互补证据，但当前音视频大语言模型可能遭受跨模态干扰：一种模态的信息误导另一种模态的解释，从而引发幻觉。我们将此问题归因于中间推理过程中不受控制的跨模态交互。为缓解此问题，我们提出“先分离后融合”（SFFL），一种旨在减少跨模态干扰的音视频推理框架。SFFL强制进行模态特定的思维链推理，生成独立的音频和视觉推理轨迹，并整合证据以回答问题。我们通过在不同模态输入设置下的数据流水线构建模态偏好标签，将这些标签作为强化学习中的辅助奖励，以鼓励在回答时对模态线索的实例依赖偏好。我们进一步引入模态特定推理机制，在分离推理阶段保持模态隔离，同时在证据融合阶段允许完全访问跨模态信息。实验表明，在准确性和鲁棒性上均有一致提升，在通用AVQA基准上平均相对增益为5.16%，在跨模态幻觉基准上为11.17%。
Summary / 总结
Current audio-visual large language models suffer from cross-modal interference, where information from one modality misguides the interpretation of another, leading to hallucinations in question answering. To address this, the authors propose Separate First, Fuse Later (SFFL), a framework that enforces modality-specific chain-of-thought reasoning to produce separate audio and visual reasoning traces before integrating evidence. They construct modality-preference labels via a data pipeline and use them as an auxiliary reward in reinforcement learning to encourage instance-dependent modality cue preference. Experiments show consistent improvements, with an average relative gain of 5.16% on general AVQA benchmarks and 11.17% on a cross-modal hallucination benchmark.
当前的音视频大语言模型在问答中常因跨模态干扰而产生幻觉，即一种模态的信息误导对另一种模态的解释。为解决此问题，作者提出“先分离后融合”（SFFL）框架，通过强制进行模态特定的思维链推理，分别生成音频和视觉推理轨迹，再整合证据。他们通过数据流水线构建模态偏好标签，并将其作为强化学习中的辅助奖励，鼓励模型根据实例依赖性地偏好模态线索。实验表明，该方法在通用AVQA基准上平均相对提升5.16%，在跨模态幻觉基准上提升11.17%，显著提高了准确性和鲁棒性。
Towards Autonomous Business Intelligence via Data-to-Insight Discovery Agent
Authors: Dongming Wu, Junwen Li, Ming Lu, Gang Wang, Ting Chen
First: 2026-05-08T03:49:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T02:23:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Transforming fragmented enterprise data into actionable insights remains a significant challenge for LLMs, constrained by complex database schemas, limitations in dynamic SQL generation, and the need for deep multi-dimensional analysis.In this paper, we propose AIDA(Autonomous Insight Discovery Agent), the first end-to-end framework designed for autonomous exploration in complex business environments. We establish a highly flexible instant retail environment encompassing 200+ metrics and 100+ dimensions, and integrates a proprietary Domain-Specific Language (DSL) that bridges semantic reasoning with precise SQL execution. Our reinforcement learning system subsequently formulates business analysis as a Pareto Principle-guided cumulative reasoning process. Experimental results demonstrate that AIDA significantly outperforms workflow-based agents, and extensive evaluations further reveal that AIDA achieves superior environmental perception and more in-depth analysis from diverse perspectives. Our work ultimately establishes the transformative potential of autonomous intelligence for industrial-scale business intelligence systems.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of transforming fragmented enterprise data into actionable insights using LLMs, which are hindered by complex schemas and limited SQL generation. The authors propose AIDA, an end-to-end framework for autonomous business intelligence, featuring a flexible retail environment with over 200 metrics and 100 dimensions, a Domain-Specific Language bridging semantic reasoning and SQL execution, and a reinforcement learning system guided by the Pareto Principle for cumulative reasoning. Experimental results show AIDA significantly outperforms workflow-based agents, achieving superior environmental perception and deeper multi-dimensional analysis, demonstrating its potential for industrial-scale business intelligence.
该论文针对利用大语言模型将碎片化企业数据转化为可执行洞察的挑战，现有方法受限于复杂数据库模式、动态SQL生成不足及深度多维分析需求。作者提出AIDA，首个面向复杂商业环境的端到端自主探索框架，构建了包含200多个指标和100多个维度的灵活零售环境，集成专有领域特定语言以桥接语义推理与精确SQL执行，并采用基于帕累托原则的强化学习系统进行累积推理。实验结果表明，AIDA显著优于基于工作流的智能体，在环境感知和多角度深度分析方面表现更佳，展示了其在工业级商业智能系统中的变革潜力。
f-GRPO and Beyond: Divergence-Based Reinforcement Learning Algorithms for General LLM Alignment
Authors: Rajdeep Haldar, Lantao Mei, Guang Lin, Yue Xing, Qifan Song
First: 2026-02-05T18:01:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T01:44:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent work shows that preference alignment objectives can be interpreted as divergence estimators between aligned (preferred) & unaligned (less-preferred) distributions, yielding a principled recipe for designing alignment losses. However, this view has so far been limited to preference-based supervision. We extend it to general LLM alignment, including reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where alignment feedback is given only as scalar rewards. We introduce $f$-Group Relative Policy Optimization ($f$-GRPO), a class of on-policy RL objectives, and $f$-Hybrid Alignment Loss ($f$-HAL), which combines on-policy reward optimization with off-policy preference supervision. We show that these objectives estimate $f$-divergences between reward-aligned & reward-unaligned distributions induced by above- & below-average reward responses, and prove expected reward improvement after alignment. Empirically, $f$-GRPO improves over GRPO on math-reasoning RLVR tasks, while hybrid $f$-HAL mitigates reward hacking in on-policy safety alignment when verifiable rewards are unavailable and learned reward models must be used.
中文标题/摘要
标题：f-GRPO及其扩展：基于散度的通用大语言模型对齐强化学习算法
近期研究表明，偏好对齐目标可解释为对齐（偏好）分布与非对齐（非偏好）分布之间的散度估计器，从而为设计对齐损失提供了原则性方法。然而，该视角目前仅限于基于偏好的监督。我们将其扩展至通用大语言模型对齐，包括可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR），其中对齐反馈仅以标量奖励形式给出。我们提出$f$-组相对策略优化（$f$-GRPO）——一类在线策略RL目标，以及$f$-混合对齐损失（$f$-HAL）——结合在线策略奖励优化与离线策略偏好监督。我们证明这些目标估计了由高于/低于平均奖励响应所诱导的奖励对齐与奖励非对齐分布之间的$f$-散度，并证明了对齐后的期望奖励提升。实验表明，在数学推理RLVR任务中，$f$-GRPO优于GRPO；而在可验证奖励不可用且必须使用学习奖励模型时，混合$f$-HAL可缓解在线策略安全对齐中的奖励破解问题。
Summary / 总结
The paper extends divergence-based alignment objectives from preference supervision to general LLM alignment, including reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). The authors propose f-Group Relative Policy Optimization (f-GRPO), a class of on-policy RL objectives, and f-Hybrid Alignment Loss (f-HAL), which combines on-policy reward optimization with off-policy preference supervision. These objectives estimate f-divergences between reward-aligned and reward-unaligned distributions, with theoretical guarantees of expected reward improvement. Empirically, f-GRPO outperforms GRPO on math-reasoning RLVR tasks, while f-HAL mitigates reward hacking in on-policy safety alignment when verifiable rewards are unavailable and learned reward models must be used.
该论文将基于散度的对齐目标从偏好监督扩展到通用大语言模型对齐，包括可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）。作者提出了f-组相对策略优化（f-GRPO），一类在线策略RL目标，以及f-混合对齐损失（f-HAL），它结合了在线策略奖励优化与离线策略偏好监督。这些目标估计奖励对齐与奖励未对齐分布之间的f-散度，并具有对齐后预期奖励提升的理论保证。实验上，f-GRPO在数学推理RLVR任务上优于GRPO，而混合f-HAL在无法获得可验证奖励且必须使用学习奖励模型时，缓解了在线策略安全对齐中的奖励黑客问题。
Exploration-Driven Optimization for Test-Time Large Language Model Reasoning
Authors: Changhao Li, Yuchen Zhuang, Chenxiao Gao, Haotian Sun, Rushi Qiang, Chao Zhang, Bo Dai
First: 2026-05-11T01:10:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-11T01:10:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted by TMLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training techniques combined with inference-time scaling significantly enhance the reasoning and alignment capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, a fundamental tension arises: inference-time methods benefit from diverse sampling from a relatively flattened probability distribution, whereas reinforcement learning (RL)-based post-training inherently sharpens these distributions. To address this, we propose Exploration-Driven Optimization (EDO), which extends reward-biasing style exploration objectives to iterative post-training and integrates them into standard RL objectives, encouraging greater diversity in sampled solutions while facilitating more effective inference-time computation. We incorporate EDO into iterative Direct Preference Optimization (iDPO) and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), resulting in two variants: ED-iDPO and ED-GRPO. Extensive experiments demonstrate that both ED-iDPO and ED-GRPO exhibit greater solution diversity and improved reasoning abilities, particularly when combined with test-time computation techniques like self-consistency. Across three in-distribution reasoning benchmarks, EDO achieves a 1.0-1.3\% improvement over the strongest baselines, and delivers an additional 1.5\% average gain on five out-of-distribution tasks. Beyond accuracy, EDO preserves model entropy and stabilizes RL training dynamics, highlighting its effectiveness in preventing over-optimization collapse. Taken together, these results establish EDO as a practical framework for balancing exploration and exploitation in LLM reasoning, especially in settings that rely on test-time scaling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探索驱动优化：面向测试时大语言模型推理的优化方法
后训练技术与推理时缩放相结合，显著提升了大型语言模型的推理与对齐能力。然而，一个根本性矛盾随之出现：推理时方法受益于从相对平坦的概率分布中进行多样化采样，而基于强化学习的后训练则天然地使这些分布趋于尖锐。为解决这一问题，我们提出探索驱动优化（EDO），将奖励偏置型探索目标扩展到迭代后训练中，并将其整合到标准强化学习目标中，从而在鼓励采样解决方案多样性的同时，促进更有效的推理时计算。我们将EDO融入迭代直接偏好优化（iDPO）和组相对策略优化（GRPO），得到两个变体：ED-iDPO和ED-GRPO。大量实验表明，ED-iDPO和ED-GRPO均展现出更高的解决方案多样性和更强的推理能力，尤其是在与自一致性等测试时计算技术结合时。在三个分布内推理基准上，EDO相比最强基线提升了1.0-1.3%，并在五个分布外任务上额外获得平均1.5%的提升。除准确性外，EDO还保持了模型熵并稳定了强化学习训练动态，凸显其在防止过度优化崩溃方面的有效性。综合来看，这些结果确立了EDO作为平衡大语言模型推理中探索与利用的实用框架，特别是在依赖测试时缩放的场景中。

Experiments show that EDO improves solution diversity and reasoning abilities, achieving a 1.0-1.3% gain over baselines on in-distribution benchmarks and an additional 1.5% average improvement on out-of-distribution tasks, while preserving model entropy and stabilizing training dynamics.
该论文针对推理时扩展需要从较平坦的概率分布中多样化采样，而基于强化学习的后训练会锐化分布这一矛盾，提出了探索驱动优化（EDO）。EDO将奖励偏置式探索目标扩展到迭代后训练中，并整合到标准强化学习目标如直接偏好优化和组相对策略优化中，形成ED-iDPO和ED-GRPO变体。实验表明，EDO提升了解决方案多样性和推理能力，在分布内基准上比最强基线提高1.0-1.3%，在分布外任务上平均额外提升1.5%，同时保持了模型熵并稳定了训练动态。
Learning to Compress Time-to-Control: A Reinforcement Learning Framework for Chronic Disease Management
Authors: Prabhjot Singh, Abhishek Gupta, Chris Betz, Abe Flansburg, Brett Ives, Sudeep Lama, Jung Hoon Son
First: 2026-05-10T23:43:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T23:43:39+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) in healthcare has had mixed results, with reward sparsity, unreliable off-policy evaluation, and deployment-simulation gap as recurring failure modes. We argue that chronic disease management is structurally a more tractable RL setting than the acute-care problems the field has primarily studied, but only if the problem is formalized to exploit chronic care's properties. We propose such a formalization. The agent's objective is to compress time-to-control (TTC) under a tiered reward calibrated to the CMS ACCESS Model. Two quantities from our companion preference-learning paper [Singh et al. 2026] enter as load-bearing structural elements: the execution intensity εbounds action availability under a constrained Markov Decision Process, and the clinician capability κweights offline-data transitions during RL training. Together they couple preference learning and RL into a two-loop architecture. We present simulation results on synthetic state machines for hypertension and type 2 diabetes. Capability-weighted offline RL outperforms uniform-weighted offline RL and the behavior policy by 15 percentage points on T2D TTC; the uniform-weighted formulation (the standard in existing healthcare RL) underperforms even the heterogeneous behavior policy. \Epsilon-aware policies generalize across deployment regimes while ε-naive policies do not.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习压缩控制时间：面向慢性病管理的强化学习框架
强化学习在医疗领域的应用结果参差不齐，奖励稀疏、离线策略评估不可靠以及部署-模拟差距是反复出现的失败模式。我们认为，慢性病管理在结构上比该领域主要研究的急性护理问题更适合强化学习，但前提是问题形式化需利用慢性护理的特性。我们提出了这样一种形式化方案。智能体的目标是在基于CMS ACCESS模型校准的分层奖励下压缩控制时间。来自我们配套偏好学习论文[Singh et al. 2026]的两个量作为关键结构要素：执行强度ε在约束马尔可夫决策过程中限制动作可用性，临床医生能力κ在强化学习训练期间对离线数据转换进行加权。两者共同将偏好学习与强化学习耦合为双循环架构。我们展示了针对高血压和2型糖尿病的合成状态机的仿真结果。能力加权离线强化学习在2型糖尿病控制时间上比均匀加权离线强化学习和行为策略高出15个百分点；均匀加权公式（现有医疗强化学习中的标准）甚至不如异质行为策略。考虑ε的策略能跨部署场景泛化，而忽略ε的策略则不能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenges of applying reinforcement learning (RL) to healthcare, such as reward sparsity and deployment-simulation gaps, by arguing that chronic disease management is more tractable than acute care if properly formalized. The authors propose a framework where the RL agent aims to compress time-to-control (TTC) using a tiered reward based on the CMS ACCESS Model, incorporating execution intensity and clinician capability from a companion preference-learning study to constrain actions and weight offline data. Simulation results on hypertension and type 2 diabetes state machines show that capability-weighted offline RL outperforms uniform-weighted RL and the behavior policy by 15 percentage points on T2D TTC, while uniform-weighted RL underperforms the behavior policy, and epsilon-aware policies generalize better than epsilon-naive ones.
该论文针对强化学习在医疗应用中面临的奖励稀疏、离线评估不可靠及部署模拟差距等挑战，提出慢性病管理在适当形式化下比急性护理更易处理。作者提出一个框架，其中强化学习智能体以压缩控制时间（TTC）为目标，采用基于CMS ACCESS模型的分层奖励，并结合来自配套偏好学习研究的执行强度和临床医生能力来约束动作和加权离线数据。在高血压和2型糖尿病状态机的模拟实验中，能力加权离线强化学习在T2D TTC上比均匀加权离线强化学习和行为策略高出15个百分点，而均匀加权公式（现有医疗强化学习标准）甚至不如异质行为策略，且感知执行强度的策略在部署场景中泛化性更好。
LEAD: Length-Efficient Adaptive and Dynamic Reasoning for Large Language Models
Authors: Songtao Wei, Yi Li, Zhikai Li, Xu Hu, Yuede Ji, Guanpeng Li, Feng Chen, Carl Yang, Zhichun Guo, Bingzhe Li
First: 2026-05-10T23:05:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T23:05:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large reasoning models, such as OpenAI o1 and DeepSeek-R1, tend to become increasingly verbose as their reasoning capabilities improve. These inflated Chain-of-Thought (CoT) trajectories often exceed what the underlying problems require, wasting compute, latency, and context budgets. While introducing length-based efficiency rewards during reinforcement learning offers a natural remedy, existing methods struggle with two fundamental challenges: the optimal balance between correctness and efficiency is non-stationary throughout training, and intrinsic reasoning budgets vary drastically across problems. Relying on static reward weights and global length constraints inevitably forces a compromise between degraded accuracy and unrealized compression. To overcome these limitations, we propose LEAD (Length-Efficient Adaptive and Dynamic reasoning), a method that replaces static heuristics with online, self-adaptive mechanisms. LEAD dynamically calibrates the correctness-efficiency trade-off at each step using a Potential-Scaled Instability, directing optimization capacity to the most informative learning signal. Furthermore, it estimates an adaptive per-problem target length online based on the model's own correct rollouts, applying a symmetric efficiency reward that penalizes both overthinking and over-compression. Evaluated on five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, LEAD achieves the highest accuracy and Accuracy-Efficiency Score among RL-trained efficient-reasoning methods while producing substantially shorter outputs than the base model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LEAD：面向大型语言模型的长度高效自适应动态推理
大型推理模型（如OpenAI o1和DeepSeek-R1）在推理能力提升的同时，往往变得愈发冗长。这些膨胀的思维链轨迹常超出问题本身所需，浪费计算、延迟和上下文预算。尽管在强化学习中引入基于长度的效率奖励是一种自然补救措施，但现有方法面临两个根本挑战：训练过程中正确性与效率之间的最优平衡是非平稳的，且不同问题的内在推理预算差异巨大。依赖静态奖励权重和全局长度约束不可避免地导致精度下降与压缩不足之间的折衷。为克服这些局限，我们提出LEAD（长度高效自适应动态推理），该方法以在线自适应机制替代静态启发式。LEAD利用势能缩放不稳定性动态校准每一步的正确性-效率权衡，将优化能力导向最具信息量的学习信号。此外，它基于模型自身的正确展开在线估计每个问题的自适应目标长度，并应用对称效率奖励，同时惩罚过度思考与过度压缩。在五个数学推理基准上的评估表明，LEAD在强化学习训练的高效推理方法中取得了最高准确率和准确率-效率得分，同时生成的输出长度显著短于基础模型。

LEAD uses Potential-Scaled Instability to dynamically calibrate the correctness-efficiency trade-off and estimates adaptive per-problem target lengths from the model's own correct rollouts, applying a symmetric efficiency reward. On five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, LEAD achieves the highest accuracy and Accuracy-Efficiency Score among RL-trained efficient-reasoning methods while generating substantially shorter outputs than the base model.
大型推理模型如OpenAI o1和DeepSeek-R1在推理能力提升时往往生成冗长的思维链，浪费计算和延迟资源。为此，作者提出LEAD方法，用在线自适应机制替代静态奖励权重。LEAD通过潜在尺度不稳定性动态校准正确性与效率的权衡，并根据模型自身的正确输出估计每个问题的自适应目标长度，施加对称效率奖励。在五个数学推理基准上，LEAD在强化学习训练的高效推理方法中取得了最高准确率和准确-效率分数，同时生成的输出比基础模型显著更短。
EvoPref: Multi-Objective Evolutionary Optimization Discovers Diverse LLM Alignments Beyond Gradient Descent
Authors: Dongxin Guo, Jikun Wu, Siu Ming Yiu
First: 2026-05-10T21:50:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:50:04+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 2 figures, 6 tables, 1 algorithm. Accepted to GECCO 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Gradient-based preference optimization methods for large language model (LLM) alignment suffer from preference collapse, converging to narrow behavioral modes while neglecting preference diversity. We introduce EvoPref, a multi-objective evolutionary algorithm that maintains populations of Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) adapters optimized across helpfulness, harmlessness, and honesty objectives using Non-dominated Sorting Genetic Algorithm II (NSGA-II) selection with archive-based diversity preservation. Our primary contribution is demonstrating that population-based methods discover substantially more diverse alignments than gradient descent. On standard benchmarks, EvoPref improves preference coverage by 18% (median 82.5% vs. 70.0% for ORPO, $p<0.001$, Wilcoxon, $n=30$) and reduces collapse rates by 47% (11.0% vs. 20.6%, $p<0.001$), while achieving competitive alignment quality (median 75.5% RewardBench vs. 75.0% for ORPO, $p<0.05$). We provide theoretical motivation extending recent multi-objective evolutionary algorithm (MOEA) runtime analysis (Dang et al., 2025) suggesting why archive-based methods escape collapse more effectively than single-trajectory optimization. Comprehensive comparisons against MOEA/D, SMS-EMOA, CMA-ES, and gradient baselines (DPO, IPO, KTO, ORPO) with rigorous statistical testing (Friedman with Holm correction, Vargha-Delaney effect sizes, median with IQR) confirm that multi-objective selection with diversity preservation is essential. This work establishes evolutionary optimization as a principled paradigm for diverse LLM alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EvoPref：多目标进化优化发现超越梯度下降的多样化大语言模型对齐
基于梯度的偏好优化方法在大语言模型对齐中面临偏好坍缩问题，即收敛到狭窄的行为模式而忽视偏好多样性。我们提出EvoPref，一种多目标进化算法，通过非支配排序遗传算法II（NSGA-II）选择与基于存档的多样性保持机制，在有用性、无害性和诚实性目标上优化低秩适配器（LoRA）种群。 我们的主要贡献在于证明基于种群的方法能发现比梯度下降显著更多样化的对齐。在标准基准测试中，EvoPref将偏好覆盖率提升18%（中位数82.5%对比ORPO的70.0%，Wilcoxon检验p<0.001，n=30），坍缩率降低47%（11.0%对比20.6%，p<0.001），同时实现具有竞争力的对齐质量（RewardBench中位数75.5%对比ORPO的75.0%，p<0.05）。我们提供理论动机，扩展近期多目标进化算法运行时分析（Dang等人，2025），表明基于存档的方法为何比单轨迹优化更有效地避免坍缩。 与MOEA/D、SMS-EMOA、CMA-ES及梯度基线方法（DPO、IPO、KTO、ORPO）的全面比较，结合严格统计检验（Holm校正的Friedman检验、Vargha-Delaney效应量、中位数与四分位距），证实了具有多样性保持的多目标选择至关重要。本工作确立了进化优化作为多样化大语言模型对齐的原则性范式。
Summary / 总结
EvoPref addresses the problem of preference collapse in gradient-based LLM alignment methods, which converge to narrow behavioral modes and neglect diversity. The method employs a multi-objective evolutionary algorithm using NSGA-II selection and archive-based diversity preservation to optimize populations of LoRA adapters across helpfulness, harmlessness, and honesty objectives. On standard benchmarks, EvoPref improves preference coverage by 18% (median 82.5% vs. 70.0% for ORPO) and reduces collapse rates by 47% (11.0% vs. 20.6%), while achieving competitive alignment quality (median 75.5% RewardBench vs. 75.0% for ORPO), with all results statistically significant. Comprehensive comparisons against MOEA/D, SMS-EMOA, CMA-ES, and gradient baselines confirm that multi-objective selection with diversity preservation is essential for discovering diverse alignments.
EvoPref针对基于梯度的LLM对齐方法中出现的偏好坍缩问题，即收敛到狭窄的行为模式而忽视偏好多样性。该方法采用多目标进化算法，利用NSGA-II选择和基于存档的多样性保持机制，优化跨有用性、无害性和诚实性目标的LoRA适配器种群。在标准基准测试中，EvoPref将偏好覆盖率提高了18%（中位数82.5%对比ORPO的70.0%），并将坍缩率降低了47%（11.0%对比20.6%），同时实现了具有竞争力的对齐质量（中位数75.5% RewardBench对比ORPO的75.0%），所有结果均具有统计显著性。与MOEA/D、SMS-EMOA、CMA-ES以及梯度基线方法的全面比较证实，结合多样性保持的多目标选择对于发现多样化的对齐至关重要。
Bayesian Optimization with Structured Measurements: A Vector-Valued RKHS Framework
Authors: Wenbin Wang, Colin N. Jones
First: 2026-05-10T21:48:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:48:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) is an efficient framework for optimizing expensive black-box functions. However, it is typically formulated as learning an end-to-end mapping from inputs to scalar objectives, thereby discarding the potentially rich information whenever a structured system output is available. In this work, we study Bayesian optimization over a vector-valued operator with structured measurements, where each measurement observes multidimensional or functional outputs, e.g., trajectories or spatial fields, rather than a single scalar value. The objective is then defined as a linear functional of these measurements. This allows each observation to reveal substantially richer information about the underlying system compared to scalar observations. Assuming the unknown operator lies in a vector-valued reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS), we derive high-probability concentration bounds for the kernel ridge regression (KRR) estimator directly in the measurement space, characterizing uncertainty in a general Hilbert space. Building on these results, we propose an algorithm based on the upper confidence bound (UCB) acquisition function with regret guarantees under mild assumptions, recovering sublinear rates for common kernels. Empirically, we demonstrate that leveraging structured measurements leads to improved sample efficiency by enabling efficient transfer of information across objectives and adaptation to time-varying settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：结构化测量的贝叶斯优化：向量值再生核希尔伯特空间框架
贝叶斯优化（BO）是优化昂贵黑箱函数的高效框架。然而，它通常被表述为从输入到标量目标的端到端映射学习，从而在结构化系统输出可用时丢弃了潜在丰富的信息。本文研究具有结构化测量的向量值算子的贝叶斯优化，其中每次测量观测多维或函数输出（例如轨迹或空间场），而非单个标量值。目标函数则定义为这些测量的线性泛函。这使得每次观测能揭示比标量观测更丰富的底层系统信息。假设未知算子属于向量值再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS），我们直接在测量空间中推导核岭回归（KRR）估计量的高概率浓度界，在一般希尔伯特空间中刻画不确定性。基于这些结果，我们提出一种基于上置信界（UCB）采集函数的算法，在温和假设下具有遗憾保证，对常见核恢复次线性收敛率。实验表明，利用结构化测量可通过跨目标高效信息迁移和适应时变设置来提升样本效率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of standard Bayesian optimization (BO) that discards rich information by only learning from scalar outputs. The authors propose a BO framework for vector-valued operators with structured measurements, such as trajectories or spatial fields, where the objective is a linear functional of these measurements. Assuming the operator lies in a vector-valued reproducing kernel Hilbert space (RKHS), they derive high-probability concentration bounds for kernel ridge regression in the measurement space and develop a UCB-based algorithm with sublinear regret guarantees. Experiments show that leveraging structured measurements improves sample efficiency through effective information transfer across objectives and adaptation to time-varying settings.
本文针对标准贝叶斯优化仅从标量输出学习而丢弃丰富信息的局限性，提出了一种面向向量值算子与结构化测量的贝叶斯优化框架，其中每次测量获得轨迹或空间场等多维或函数输出，目标函数定义为这些测量的线性泛函。假设算子位于向量值再生核希尔伯特空间中，作者推导了测量空间中核岭回归估计的高概率置信界，并基于置信上界采集函数设计了具有次线性遗憾保证的算法。实验表明，利用结构化测量可通过跨目标的信息高效迁移和对时变环境的适应来提升样本效率。
Efficient Estimation of Kernel Surrogate Models for Task Attribution
Authors: Zhenshuo Zhang, Minxuan Duan, Hongyang R. Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-03T17:43:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:29:30+00:00
Comments: 27 pages. Appeared in ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern AI agents such as large language models are trained on diverse tasks -- translation, code generation, mathematical reasoning, and text prediction -- simultaneously. A key question is how to quantify the influence of each individual training task on performance on a target task, a problem we refer to as task attribution. The direct approach, leave-one-out retraining, measures the effect of removing each task, but is computationally infeasible at scale. An alternative approach that builds surrogate models to predict the performance on a target task for any subset of training tasks has emerged in the recent literature. Prior work focuses on linear surrogate models, which capture first-order relationships but miss nonlinear interactions such as XOR-type effects. In this paper, we first consider a unified task-weighting framework for analyzing task-attribution methods and establish a new connection between linear surrogate models and influence functions via a second-order analysis. Then, we introduce kernel surrogate models, which more effectively represent second-order task interactions. To efficiently learn the kernel surrogate, we develop a gradient-based estimation procedure that leverages a first-order approximation of pretrained models; empirically, this yields accurate surrogate estimates with less than $2\%$ relative error without repeated retraining. Experiments across multiple settings -- including mathematical reasoning in transformers, in-context learning, and multi-objective reinforcement learning -- demonstrate the effectiveness of kernel surrogate models. They achieve a $25\%$ higher correlation with the leave-one-out ground truth than linear surrogates and influence-function baselines, enabling more accurate and scalable task attribution. When used for downstream data selection, kernel surrogate models further yield a $40\%$ improvement in the aforementioned settings.

标题：用于任务归因的核代理模型的高效估计
现代AI智能体（如大型语言模型）同时针对多种任务进行训练——翻译、代码生成、数学推理和文本预测。一个关键问题是如何量化每个单独训练任务对目标任务性能的影响，我们称之为任务归因。直接方法（留一法重新训练）衡量移除每个任务的效果，但在大规模场景下计算不可行。近期文献中出现了一种替代方法，即构建代理模型来预测任意训练任务子集在目标任务上的性能。先前的工作侧重于线性代理模型，这类模型能捕捉一阶关系，但忽略了非线性交互（如XOR型效应）。本文首先考虑一个统一的任务加权框架来分析任务归因方法，并通过二阶分析建立线性代理模型与影响函数之间的新联系。接着，我们引入核代理模型，它能更有效地表示二阶任务交互。为了高效学习核代理，我们开发了一种基于梯度的估计程序，利用预训练模型的一阶近似；实验表明，该方法无需重复训练即可获得相对误差低于2%的准确代理估计。在多个场景（包括Transformer中的数学推理、上下文学习和多目标强化学习）中的实验证明了核代理模型的有效性。与线性代理和影响函数基线相比，核代理模型与留一法真实值的相关性提高了25%，实现了更准确且可扩展的任务归因。当用于下游数据选择时，核代理模型在上述场景中进一步带来了40%的性能提升。

They develop a gradient-based estimation procedure using a first-order approximation of pretrained models, achieving less than 2% relative error without repeated retraining. Experiments on mathematical reasoning, in-context learning, and multi-objective reinforcement learning show that kernel surrogates achieve 25% higher correlation with leave-one-out ground truth than linear surrogates and influence functions, and yield a 40% improvement in downstream data selection tasks.

Can RL Teach Long-Horizon Reasoning to LLMs? Expressiveness Is Key
Authors: Tianle Wang, Zhaoyang Wang, Guangchen Lan, Xinpeng Wei, Sipeng Zhang, Guanwen Qiu, Abulhair Saparov
First: 2026-05-07T17:48:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T20:28:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has been applied to improve large language model (LLM) reasoning, yet the systematic study of how training scales with task difficulty has been hampered by the lack of controlled, scalable environments. Observed LLM shortcomings in long-horizon reasoning have raised the prospect that these shortcomings are fundamental to the autoregressive transformer architecture. We introduce ScaleLogic, a synthetic logical reasoning framework that offers independent control over two axes of difficulty: the depth of the required proof planning (i.e., the horizon) and the expressiveness of the underlying logic. Our proposed framework supports a wide range of logics: from simple implication-only logic ("if-then") towards more expressive first-order reasoning with conjunction ("and"), disjunction ("or"), negation ("not"), and universal quantification ("for all"). Using this framework, we show that the RL training compute $T$ follows a power law with respect to reasoning depth $D$ ($T \propto D^γ$, $R^{2} > 0.99$), and that the scaling exponent $γ$ increases monotonically with logical expressiveness, from $1.04$ to $2.60$. On downstream mathematics and general reasoning benchmarks, more expressive training settings yield both larger performance gains (up to $+10.66$ points) and more compute-efficient transfer compared to less expressive settings, demonstrating that what a model is trained on, not just how much it is trained, shapes downstream transfer. We further show that the power-law relationship holds across multiple RL methods, and curriculum-based training substantially improves scaling efficiency. More broadly, our results demonstrate that LLM shortcomings in long-horizon reasoning are not fundamental to the underlying architecture, and can be addressed by improved training methodology and data.
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether reinforcement learning (RL) can teach large language models (LLMs) long-horizon reasoning, motivated by concerns that autoregressive transformers may fundamentally struggle with such tasks. To systematically study this, the authors introduce ScaleLogic, a synthetic logical reasoning framework that independently controls reasoning depth and logical expressiveness, ranging from simple implication to first-order logic. Their experiments show that RL training compute follows a power law with respect to reasoning depth, with the scaling exponent increasing monotonically from 1.04 to 2.60 as expressiveness grows. On downstream benchmarks, more expressive training settings yield up to +10.66 points improvement and better compute efficiency, demonstrating that LLM shortcomings in long-horizon reasoning are not architectural but can be mitigated by improved training methodology and data.
该论文探讨强化学习能否教会大语言模型进行长程推理，其动机源于对自回归Transformer架构可能根本性难以处理此类任务的担忧。为系统研究这一问题，作者提出了ScaleLogic，一个合成逻辑推理框架，可独立控制推理深度和逻辑表达能力（从简单蕴含到一阶逻辑）。实验表明，强化学习训练计算量随推理深度呈幂律增长，且缩放指数随表达能力增强从1.04单调增至2.60。在下游基准测试中，更具表达能力的训练设置带来高达+10.66分的性能提升和更高的计算效率，证明大语言模型在长程推理上的不足并非架构固有，而是可以通过改进训练方法和数据来克服。
One for All: A Non-Linear Transformer can Enable Cross-Domain Generalization for In-Context Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Bowen He, Juncheng Dong, Lin Lin, Xiang Cheng
First: 2026-05-10T19:52:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T19:52:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL) is to learn models that generalize beyond the tasks on which they are trained, a goal traditionally pursued through multi-task and meta RL. Recently, transformer architectures have emerged as a promising approach, enabling adaptation to new tasks via in-context learning without explicit parameter updates. From a functional perspective, a transformer can be viewed as a functional operator that maps a context to a task-specific function. It is thus fundamental to understand and design this operator to support stronger generalization in RL. In this work, we address this resulting question of generalization from a kernel-based perspective by establishing a connection between non-linear transformers and kernel-based temporal difference learning. By interpreting the transformer as performing regression in a Reproducing Kernel Hilbert Space (RKHS), we show that value functions from different domains can be represented using a shared set of weights, provided they lie within the same RKHS. Experiments on multiple MetaWorld domains support this interpretation, demonstrating convergence of the temporal-difference objective.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一统天下：非线性Transformer可实现跨域泛化的上下文强化学习
强化学习（RL）的核心挑战之一是学习能够泛化到训练任务之外的模型，这一目标传统上通过多任务和元RL来实现。近年来，Transformer架构作为一种有前景的方法出现，能够通过上下文学习适应新任务，而无需显式参数更新。从功能角度看，Transformer可视为将上下文映射到特定任务函数的函数算子。因此，理解并设计该算子以支持RL中更强的泛化能力至关重要。在本工作中，我们从核方法视角出发，通过建立非线性Transformer与基于核的时序差分学习之间的联系，来解决这一泛化问题。通过将Transformer解释为在再生核希尔伯特空间（RKHS）中进行回归，我们证明不同域的值函数若位于同一RKHS中，则可用共享权重集表示。在多个MetaWorld域上的实验支持了这一解释，并展示了时序差分目标函数的收敛性。

Adaptive Data Harvesting for Efficient Neural Network Learning with Universal Constraints
Authors: Siteng Kang, Xinhua Zhang
First: 2026-05-10T19:09:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T19:09:49+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training neural networks to satisfy universal constraints over continuous domains poses unique challenges. Common examples include Lyapunov Neural Networks (Lyapunov NNs) and Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs), where analytical solutions are generally either unavailable or overly restrictive. Sample-based methods are therefore commonly used to enforce these constraints, and the choice of samples has a substantial impact on convergence speed, stability, and solution quality. Most existing methods rely on fixed heuristics or handcrafted rules, and are suboptimal in practice. In this paper, we aim to improve upon them by learning, from data and experience, how to dynamically and iteratively adjust the samples in response to the model's evolving learning performance. Trained by reinforcement learning, the learned policy improves empirical constraint satisfaction on test problems while significantly improving efficiency. We validate the approach on both Lyapunov NNs and PINNs, and demonstrate its broader applicability to domains where adaptive input selection is essential for effective training.

标题：面向通用约束的高效神经网络学习的自适应数据采集
训练神经网络以满足连续域上的通用约束面临独特挑战。常见例子包括李雅普诺夫神经网络和物理信息神经网络，其中解析解通常不可用或过于严格。因此，基于样本的方法常被用于强制执行这些约束，而样本的选择对收敛速度、稳定性和解质量有显著影响。现有方法大多依赖固定启发式或手工规则，在实践中并非最优。本文旨在通过从数据和经验中学习如何根据模型不断变化的学习性能动态迭代调整样本，从而改进这些方法。通过强化学习训练，所学策略在测试问题上提高了经验约束满足度，同时显著提升了效率。我们在李雅普诺夫神经网络和物理信息神经网络上验证了该方法，并展示了其在自适应输入选择对有效训练至关重要的领域的更广泛适用性。

Q-learning with Adjoint Matching
Authors: Qiyang Li, Sergey Levine
First: 2026-01-20T18:45:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T18:34:25+00:00
Comments: 32 pages, 8 figures, 7 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose Q-learning with Adjoint Matching (QAM), a novel TD-based reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that tackles a long-standing challenge in continuous-action RL: efficient optimization of an expressive diffusion or flow-matching policy with respect to a parameterized Q-function. Effective optimization requires exploiting the first-order information of the critic, but it is challenging to do so for flow or diffusion policies because direct gradient-based optimization via backpropagation through their multi-step denoising process is numerically unstable. Existing methods work around this either by only using the value and discarding the gradient information, or by relying on approximations that sacrifice policy expressivity or bias the learned policy. QAM sidesteps both of these challenges by leveraging adjoint matching, a recently proposed technique in generative modeling, which transforms the critic's action gradient to form a step-wise objective function that is free from unstable backpropagation, while providing an unbiased, expressive policy at the optimum. Combined with temporal-difference backup for critic learning, QAM consistently outperforms prior approaches on hard, sparse reward tasks in both offline and offline-to-online RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：伴随匹配Q学习
我们提出伴随匹配Q学习（QAM），一种基于时序差分（TD）的新型强化学习（RL）算法，旨在解决连续动作强化学习中的长期挑战：如何高效优化一个表达力强的扩散或流匹配策略，使其与参数化Q函数相匹配。有效优化需要利用评论家的一阶信息，但对于流或扩散策略而言，通过其多步去噪过程进行基于梯度的反向传播优化在数值上不稳定，因此极具挑战性。现有方法要么仅使用值函数而丢弃梯度信息，要么依赖牺牲策略表达力或引入偏差的近似方法。QAM通过利用生成建模中最新提出的伴随匹配技术，将评论家的动作梯度转化为逐步目标函数，避免了不稳定的反向传播，同时在最优解处提供无偏且表达力强的策略。结合用于评论家学习的时序差分备份，QAM在离线及离线到在线强化学习的困难稀疏奖励任务中持续优于先前方法。
