QAM addresses this by leveraging adjoint matching from generative modeling, which transforms the critic's action gradient into a step-wise objective that avoids unstable backpropagation while maintaining an unbiased and expressive policy at the optimum. Combined with temporal-difference learning for the critic, QAM consistently outperforms prior methods on hard, sparse reward tasks in both offline and offline-to-online RL settings, as demonstrated by experimental results.
该论文提出了Q-learning with Adjoint Matching (QAM)，一种新颖的强化学习算法，旨在高效优化连续动作空间中的扩散或流匹配策略，这类策略因多步去噪过程的反向传播数值不稳定而难以优化。QAM通过利用生成建模中的伴随匹配技术，将评论家的动作梯度转化为逐步目标函数，避免了不稳定的反向传播，同时在最优解处保持无偏且表达力强的策略。结合时序差分学习来更新评论家，QAM在离线及离线到在线强化学习的困难稀疏奖励任务中，始终优于先前方法，实验结果验证了其有效性。
Knowledge is Not Enough: Injecting RL Skills for Continual Adaptation
Authors: Pingzhi Tang, Yiding Wang, Muhan Zhang
First: 2026-01-16T13:08:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T17:10:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) face the "knowledge cutoff" challenge, where their frozen parametric memory prevents direct internalization of new information. While Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) is commonly used to update model knowledge, it often updates factual content without reliably improving the model's ability to use the newly incorporated information for question answering or decision-making. Reinforcement Learning (RL) is essential for acquiring reasoning skills; however, its high computational cost makes it impractical for efficient online adaptation. We empirically observe that the parameter updates induced by SFT and RL are nearly orthogonal. Based on this observation, we propose Parametric Skill Transfer (PaST), a framework that supports modular skill transfer for efficient and effective knowledge adaptation. By extracting a domain-agnostic Skill Vector from a source domain, we can linearly inject knowledge manipulation skills into a target model after it has undergone lightweight SFT on new data. Experiments on knowledge-incorporation QA (SQuAD, LooGLE) and agentic tool-use benchmarks (ToolBench) demonstrate the effectiveness of our method. On SQuAD, PaST outperforms the state-of-the-art self-editing SFT baseline by up to 9.9 points. PaST further scales to long-context QA on LooGLE with an 8.0-point absolute accuracy gain, and improves zero-shot ToolBench success rates by +10.3 points on average with consistent gains across tool categories, indicating strong scalability and cross-domain transferability of the Skill Vector.
中文标题/摘要
标题：知识不足：注入强化学习技能以实现持续适应
大型语言模型面临“知识截止”挑战，其冻结的参数化记忆阻止了直接内化新信息。虽然监督微调常用于更新模型知识，但它往往更新事实内容，却未能可靠提升模型利用新信息进行问答或决策的能力。强化学习对于获取推理技能至关重要，但其高计算成本使其不适用于高效的在线适应。我们通过实验观察到，SFT和RL引起的参数更新几乎正交。基于此观察，我们提出参数化技能迁移框架，支持模块化技能迁移以实现高效且有效的知识适应。通过从源领域提取领域无关的技能向量，我们可以在目标模型对新数据进行轻量级SFT后，线性注入知识操作技能。在知识整合问答和智能体工具使用基准上的实验证明了我们方法的有效性。在SQuAD上，PaST比最先进的自编辑SFT基线高出最多9.9分。PaST进一步扩展到LooGLE上的长上下文问答，绝对准确率提升8.0分，并在ToolBench上将零样本成功率平均提高+10.3分，且各工具类别表现一致，表明技能向量具有强可扩展性和跨领域迁移性。
Summary / 总结
Large Language Models suffer from a knowledge cutoff, and while Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) can update factual content, it fails to improve the model's reasoning skills for using new information, whereas Reinforcement Learning (RL) is effective for acquiring such skills but is computationally prohibitive for online adaptation. Observing that SFT and RL parameter updates are nearly orthogonal, the authors propose Parametric Skill Transfer (PaST), which extracts a domain-agnostic Skill Vector from a source domain via RL and linearly injects it into a target model after lightweight SFT on new data. Experiments on SQuAD, LooGLE, and ToolBench show PaST outperforms the state-of-the-art SFT baseline by up to 9.9 points on SQuAD, achieves an 8.0-point absolute accuracy gain on LooGLE, and improves zero-shot ToolBench success rates by +10.3 points on average, demonstrating strong scalability and cross-domain transferability.
大型语言模型面临知识截止问题，监督微调虽能更新事实内容，但无法提升模型运用新信息进行推理的技能，而强化学习虽能有效获取推理能力，但其高计算成本使其不适用于高效在线适应。基于监督微调和强化学习的参数更新近乎正交的观察，作者提出参数化技能迁移框架，通过从源领域提取领域无关的技能向量，在目标模型经轻量监督微调后线性注入该向量。在SQuAD、LooGLE和ToolBench上的实验表明，该方法在SQuAD上比最先进的监督微调基线高出最多9.9分，在LooGLE上获得8.0个百分点的绝对准确率提升，并在ToolBench上将零样本成功率平均提高10.3个百分点，展现出强大的可扩展性和跨领域迁移能力。
Impact of Connectivity on Laplacian Representations in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tommaso Giorgi, Pierriccardo Olivieri, Keyue Jiang, Laura Toni, Matteo Papini
First: 2026-03-09T16:20:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T16:34:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning compact state representations in Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) has proven crucial for addressing the curse of dimensionality in large-scale reinforcement learning (RL) problems. Existing principled approaches leverage structural priors on the MDP by constructing state representations as linear combinations of the state-graph Laplacian eigenvectors. When the transition graph is unknown or the state space is prohibitively large, the graph spectral features can be estimated directly via sample trajectories. In this work, we prove an upper bound on the approximation error of linear value function approximation under the learned spectral features. We show how this error scales with the algebraic connectivity of the state-graph, grounding the approximation quality in the topological structure of the MDP. We further bound the error introduced by the eigenvector estimation itself, leading to an end-to-end error decomposition across the representation learning pipeline. Additionally, our expression of the Laplacian operator for the RL setting, although equivalent to existing ones, prevents some common misunderstandings, of which we show some examples from the literature. Our results hold for general (non-uniform) policies without any assumptions on the symmetry of the induced transition kernel. We validate our theoretical findings with numerical simulations on gridworld environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连通性对强化学习中拉普拉斯表示的影响
在马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中学习紧凑的状态表示，对于解决大规模强化学习（RL）问题中的维度灾难至关重要。现有原则性方法通过将状态图拉普拉斯特征向量的线性组合作为状态表示，利用MDP的结构先验。当转移图未知或状态空间过大时，可通过样本轨迹直接估计图谱特征。本文证明了在所学谱特征下线性值函数逼近的近似误差上界，展示了该误差如何随状态图的代数连通性变化，从而将逼近质量与MDP拓扑结构联系起来。进一步界定了特征向量估计本身引入的误差，形成了表示学习流水线的端到端误差分解。此外，本文对RL场景中拉普拉斯算子的表达式虽与现有形式等价，但能避免常见误解，并列举了文献中的实例。我们的结论适用于一般（非均匀）策略，无需对诱导转移核的对称性作任何假设。通过网格世界环境的数值模拟验证了理论发现。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how the connectivity of the state-transition graph affects the quality of Laplacian-based state representations in reinforcement learning. The authors derive an upper bound on the approximation error of linear value functions using learned spectral features, showing that the error scales with the algebraic connectivity of the graph. They also bound the error from eigenvector estimation, providing an end-to-end error decomposition. Numerical simulations on gridworld environments validate the theoretical results, demonstrating that better-connected graphs yield more accurate value function approximation.
本文研究了状态转移图的连通性如何影响基于拉普拉斯算子的状态表示在强化学习中的质量。作者推导了使用学习到的谱特征进行线性值函数逼近的误差上界，表明该误差与状态图的代数连通性成比例。他们还对特征向量估计引入的误差进行了界定，提供了端到端的误差分解。在网格世界环境中的数值模拟验证了理论结果，表明连通性更好的图能带来更精确的值函数逼近。
Plan2Cleanse: Test-Time Backdoor Defense via Monte-Carlo Planning in Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Sze-Ann Chen, Zhi-Yi Chin, Kui-Yuan Chen, Chi-Yu Li, Ping-Chun Hsieh
First: 2026-05-10T16:34:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T16:34:16+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Ensuring the security of reinforcement learning (RL) models is critical, particularly when they are trained by third parties and deployed in real-world systems. Attackers can implant backdoors into these models, causing them to behave normally under typical conditions, but execute malicious behaviors when specific triggers are activated. In this work, we propose Plan2Cleanse, a test-time detection and mitigation framework that adapts Monte Carlo Tree Search to efficiently identify and neutralize RL backdoor attacks without requiring model retraining. Our approach recasts backdoor detection as a planning problem, enabling systematic exploration of temporally extended trigger sequences while maintaining black-box access to the target policy. By leveraging the detection results, Plan2Cleanse can further achieve efficient mitigation through tree-search preventive replanning. We evaluated our method in competitive MuJoCo environments, simulated O-RAN wireless networks, and Atari games. Plan2Cleanse achieves substantial improvements, increasing trigger detection success rates by more than 61.4 percentage points in stealthy O-RAN scenarios and improving win rates from 35\% to 53\% in competitive Humanoid environments. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of our test-time defense approach and highlight the importance of proactive defenses against backdoor threats in RL deployments. Our implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/rl-bandits-lab/RL-Backdoor.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Plan2Cleanse：基于蒙特卡洛规划的深度强化学习测试时后门防御
确保强化学习模型的安全性至关重要，尤其是当它们由第三方训练并部署在现实系统中时。攻击者可能在这些模型中植入后门，使其在正常情况下表现正常，但在特定触发器激活时执行恶意行为。本文提出Plan2Cleanse，一种测试时检测与缓解框架，通过适配蒙特卡洛树搜索高效识别并消除强化学习后门攻击，无需重新训练模型。该方法将后门检测重新定义为规划问题，在保持对目标策略黑盒访问的同时，系统性地探索时间扩展的触发器序列。利用检测结果，Plan2Cleanse可通过基于树搜索的预防性重规划实现高效缓解。我们在竞争性MuJoCo环境、模拟O-RAN无线网络及Atari游戏中评估了该方法。Plan2Cleanse在隐蔽O-RAN场景中将触发器检测成功率提升超过61.4个百分点，在竞争性Humanoid环境中将胜率从35%提升至53%。这些结果证明了测试时防御方法的有效性，并凸显了在强化学习部署中主动防御后门威胁的重要性。我们的实现已公开于https://github.com/rl-bandits-lab/RL-Backdoor。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes Plan2Cleanse, a test-time backdoor defense framework for deep reinforcement learning that uses Monte Carlo Tree Search to detect and mitigate attacks without retraining. The method reformulates backdoor detection as a planning problem, allowing systematic exploration of trigger sequences under black-box access, and achieves mitigation through tree-search preventive replanning. Evaluated on MuJoCo, O-RAN wireless networks, and Atari games, Plan2Cleanse improves trigger detection success rates by over 61.4 percentage points in stealthy O-RAN scenarios and boosts win rates from 35% to 53% in competitive Humanoid environments, demonstrating its effectiveness.
该论文提出Plan2Cleanse，一种针对深度强化学习的测试时后门防御框架，利用蒙特卡洛树搜索在不重新训练模型的情况下检测并缓解攻击。该方法将后门检测重新定义为规划问题，在黑盒访问下系统性地探索时间扩展的触发序列，并通过树搜索预防性重规划实现高效缓解。在MuJoCo、O-RAN无线网络和Atari游戏上的评估显示，Plan2Cleanse在隐蔽的O-RAN场景中将触发检测成功率提升超过61.4个百分点，并在竞争性Humanoid环境中将胜率从35%提高到53%，证明了其有效性。
Auction-Based Online Policy Adaptation for Evolving Objectives
Authors: Guruprerana Shabadi, Kaushik Mallik
First: 2026-04-02T15:17:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T16:27:29+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider multi-objective reinforcement learning problems where objectives come from an identical family -- such as the class of reachability objectives -- and may appear or disappear at runtime. Our goal is to design adaptive policies that can efficiently adjust their behaviors as the set of active objectives changes. To solve this problem, we propose a modular framework where each objective is supported by a selfish local policy, and coordination is achieved through a novel auction-based mechanism: policies bid for the right to execute their actions, with bids reflecting the urgency of the current state. The highest bidder selects the action, enabling a dynamic and interpretable trade-off among objectives. Going back to the original adaptation problem, when objectives change, the system adapts by simply adding or removing the corresponding policies. Moreover, as objectives arise from the same family, identical copies of a parameterized policy can be deployed, facilitating immediate adaptation at runtime. We show how the selfish local policies can be computed by turning the problem into a general-sum Markov game, where the policies compete against each other to fulfill their own objectives. To succeed, each policy must not only optimize its own objective, but also reason about the presence of other goals and learn to produce calibrated bids that reflect relative priority. Under mild assumptions, we prove the existence of Nash equilibria where dishonest bidding leads to suboptimal outcome, and the most urgent objectives win control automatically. In our implementation, the policies are trained concurrently using proximal policy optimization (PPO). We evaluate on two Atari games and a gridworld-based path-planning task with dynamic targets. Our method achieves substantially better performance than monolithic policies trained with PPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于拍卖的在线策略适应以应对动态目标
我们考虑多目标强化学习问题，其中目标来自同一家族（例如可达性目标类），并可能在运行时出现或消失。我们的目标是设计自适应策略，使其能够随着活跃目标集的变化高效调整行为。为解决此问题，我们提出一个模块化框架：每个目标由一个自私的局部策略支持，并通过一种新颖的基于拍卖的机制实现协调——策略竞标执行其动作的权利，出价反映当前状态的紧迫性。最高出价者选择动作，从而实现目标间动态且可解释的权衡。回到原始适应问题，当目标变化时，系统通过简单地添加或移除相应策略来适应。此外，由于目标来自同一家族，可部署参数化策略的相同副本，从而促进运行时即时适应。我们展示了如何通过将问题转化为一般和马尔可夫博弈来计算自私的局部策略，其中策略相互竞争以实现各自目标。为了成功，每个策略不仅需优化自身目标，还需考虑其他目标的存在，并学习生成反映相对优先级的校准出价。在温和假设下，我们证明了纳什均衡的存在性，其中不诚实出价导致次优结果，而最紧迫的目标自动获得控制权。在我们的实现中，策略使用近端策略优化（PPO）进行并发训练。我们在两个Atari游戏和一个具有动态目标的基于网格世界的路径规划任务上进行了评估。我们的方法比使用PPO训练的单一策略取得了显著更好的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses multi-objective reinforcement learning where objectives from the same family, such as reachability goals, can appear or disappear at runtime, requiring adaptive policies. The authors propose a modular framework where each objective is handled by a selfish local policy, and coordination is achieved via an auction-based mechanism where policies bid for action execution based on urgency. The problem is formulated as a general-sum Markov game, and policies are trained concurrently with PPO, with theoretical guarantees that dishonest bidding leads to suboptimal outcomes. Experiments on two Atari games and a gridworld path-planning task show that the proposed method significantly outperforms monolithic PPO policies.
本文针对多目标强化学习中目标来自同一家族（如可达性目标）且可能在运行时出现或消失的问题，提出了一种自适应策略设计方法。作者构建了一个模块化框架，每个目标由自私的局部策略支持，并通过新颖的拍卖机制实现协调：策略根据当前状态的紧迫性进行出价，出价最高者选择动作。该问题被转化为一般和马尔可夫博弈，策略使用PPO算法并行训练，理论证明不诚实出价会导致次优结果。在两项Atari游戏和一项网格世界路径规划任务上的实验表明，该方法显著优于使用PPO训练的单一策略。
Any2Any 3D Diffusion Models with Knowledge Transfer: A Radiotherapy Planning Study
Authors: Yuhan Wang, Zihan Li, Han Liu, Simon Arberet, Martin Kraus, Yuyin Zhou, Florin-Cristian Ghesu, Dorin Comaniciu, Ali Kamen, Riqiang Gao
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-05-10T16:08:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T16:08:36+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026 main conference. Compare to CVPR version, minor updates here are included (e.g., combine main text and appendix; clarify the timing scenario in appendix)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Voxel-wise dose prediction is a critical yet challenging task in practical radiotherapy (RT) planning, as bespoke models trained from scratch often struggle to generalize across diverse clinical settings. Meanwhile, generative models trained on billion-scale datasets from vision domains have achieved impressive performance. Herein, we propose DiffKT3D, a unified Any2Any 3D diffusion framework that leverages prior knowledge from pretrained video diffusion models for efficient and clinically meaningful dose prediction. To enable flexible conditioning across multiple clinical modalities (CT, anatomical structures, body, beam settings, etc.), we introduce an Any2Any conditional paradigm utilizing modality-specific embeddings without cross-attention overhead. Further, we design a novel reinforcement learning (RL) post-training mechanism guided by a clinically-informed Scorecard explicitly tailored to institutional treatment preferences. Compared with winner of GDP-HMM challenge, DiffKT3D sets a new state-of-the-art in dose prediction by reducing voxel-level MAE from 2.07 to 1.93. In addition, DiffKT3D achieves superior image quality and preference match. These results demonstrate that transferring diffusion priors via modality-aware conditioning and clinically aligned RL post-training can provide a robust and generalizable solution for RT planning across various clinical scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于知识迁移的任意到任意三维扩散模型：一项放射治疗计划研究
体素级剂量预测是实际放射治疗（RT）计划中一项关键但具有挑战性的任务，因为从头训练的定制模型往往难以泛化到不同的临床环境。与此同时，在视觉领域数十亿规模数据集上训练的生成模型已取得令人瞩目的性能。为此，我们提出DiffKT3D，一个统一的任意到任意三维扩散框架，利用预训练视频扩散模型的先验知识，实现高效且具有临床意义的剂量预测。为了支持跨多种临床模态（CT、解剖结构、体部、射束设置等）的灵活条件控制，我们引入了一种任意到任意条件范式，利用模态特定嵌入，无需交叉注意力开销。此外，我们设计了一种新颖的强化学习（RL）后训练机制，由临床知情评分卡引导，该评分卡明确针对机构治疗偏好定制。与GDP-HMM挑战赛的获胜者相比，DiffKT3D将体素级平均绝对误差从2.07降至1.93，在剂量预测中树立了新的最先进水平。此外，DiffKT3D在图像质量和偏好匹配方面表现更优。这些结果表明，通过模态感知条件控制和临床对齐的RL后训练迁移扩散先验，可以为各种临床场景下的RT计划提供稳健且可泛化的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of voxel-wise dose prediction in radiotherapy planning, where models trained from scratch often fail to generalize across diverse clinical settings. The authors propose DiffKT3D, a unified Any2Any 3D diffusion framework that transfers knowledge from pretrained video diffusion models to enable efficient and clinically meaningful dose prediction. To handle flexible conditioning on multiple clinical modalities, they introduce an Any2Any conditional paradigm using modality-specific embeddings without cross-attention overhead, and a reinforcement learning post-training mechanism guided by a clinically-informed Scorecard. Experimental results show that DiffKT3D achieves state-of-the-art performance, reducing voxel-level MAE from 2.07 to 1.93 compared to the winner of the GDP-HMM challenge, while also delivering superior image quality and preference match.
本文针对放射治疗计划中体素级剂量预测的挑战，即从头训练的模型难以泛化到不同临床场景。作者提出DiffKT3D，一个统一的Any2Any 3D扩散框架，通过迁移预训练视频扩散模型的知识，实现高效且临床有意义的剂量预测。为处理多种临床模态的灵活条件输入，他们引入了一种无需交叉注意力的Any2Any条件范式，使用模态特定嵌入，并设计了一种基于临床知情评分卡的强化学习后训练机制。实验结果表明，DiffKT3D达到了最先进性能，与GDP-HMM挑战赛冠军相比，将体素级平均绝对误差从2.07降至1.93，同时实现了更优的图像质量和偏好匹配。
Neuromorphic Reinforcement Learning for Quadruped Locomotion Control on Uneven Terrain
Authors: Zhuangyu Han, Abhronil Sengupta
First: 2026-05-10T15:16:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T15:16:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has enabled robust quadruped locomotion over complex terrain, but most learned controllers are trained offline with backpropagation in massively parallel simulation and deployed as fixed policies, limiting adaptation to terrain variation, payload changes, actuator wear, and other real-world conditions under onboard power constraints. Local learning provides a potential path toward energy-aware on-robot adaptation by replacing global backpropagation graphs with updates driven by local neural states, making the learning rule more compatible with neuromorphic and in-memory computing substrates. This work proposes an equilibrium-propagation (EP)-based proximal policy optimization (PPO) framework for uneven-terrain quadruped locomotion. The controller combines a bio-inspired central pattern generator (CPG) policy with a residual postural adjustment policy, while replacing conventional backpropagation-trained policy and value networks with EP-enabled local learning. To train stochastic continuous-control policies with EP, we derive an EP-compatible PPO output-nudging signal and introduce a two-sided ratio clipping mechanism that stabilizes policy updates during relaxation. Experiments on a 12-DoF A1 quadruped show that the proposed controller achieves stable policy convergence in a two-stage uneven terrain locomotion task. Its locomotion performance is comparable to a backpropagation-trained PPO baseline in success rate, velocity tracking, actuator power, and body stability, while improving GPU memory efficiency by 4.3\(\times\) compared with backpropagation through time (BPTT). These results suggest that local equilibrium-based learning can support high-dimensional embodied locomotion and provide an algorithmic foundation for low-power on-robot adaptation and fine-tuning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向不平地形四足运动控制的神经形态强化学习
强化学习（RL）已能在复杂地形上实现稳健的四足运动，但大多数学习控制器是通过大规模并行仿真中的反向传播进行离线训练，并作为固定策略部署，这限制了其在机载功耗约束下对地形变化、负载变化、执行器磨损及其他现实条件的适应能力。局部学习通过用局部神经状态驱动的更新替代全局反向传播图，为能量感知的机器人自适应提供了潜在路径，使学习规则更兼容神经形态和内存计算基底。本文提出了一种基于平衡传播（EP）的近端策略优化（PPO）框架，用于不平地形四足运动。该控制器结合了仿生中枢模式发生器（CPG）策略与残余姿态调整策略，同时用支持EP的局部学习替代了传统反向传播训练的策略和价值网络。为通过EP训练随机连续控制策略，我们推导了EP兼容的PPO输出扰动信号，并引入了一种双边比率裁剪机制，在松弛过程中稳定策略更新。在12自由度A1四足机器人上的实验表明，所提控制器能在两阶段不平地形运动任务中实现稳定的策略收敛。其运动性能在成功率、速度跟踪、执行器功率和身体稳定性方面与反向传播训练的PPO基线相当，同时与通过时间反向传播（BPTT）相比，GPU内存效率提升了4.3倍。这些结果表明，基于局部平衡的学习可支持高维具身运动，并为低功耗机载自适应和微调提供了算法基础。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of enabling energy-efficient on-robot adaptation for quadruped locomotion on uneven terrain, motivated by the limitations of offline-trained reinforcement learning controllers that lack adaptability and consume high power. The authors propose a neuromorphic reinforcement learning framework that combines equilibrium-propagation (EP) with proximal policy optimization (PPO), using a bio-inspired central pattern generator policy and a residual postural adjustment policy, while replacing traditional backpropagation with EP-based local learning for policy and value networks. Experimental results on a 12-DoF A1 quadruped demonstrate that the proposed controller achieves stable policy convergence and comparable locomotion performance to a backpropagation-trained PPO baseline in success rate, velocity tracking, actuator power, and body stability, while improving GPU memory efficiency by 4.3 times compared to backpropagation through time.
本文针对四足机器人在不平坦地形上实现低功耗在线自适应的问题，提出了一种基于平衡传播（EP）的邻近策略优化（PPO）框架，结合生物启发的中央模式发生器策略和残余姿态调整策略，用EP局部学习替代传统反向传播来训练策略网络和价值网络。在12自由度A1四足机器人上的实验表明，该控制器在两级不平坦地形运动任务中实现了稳定的策略收敛，在成功率、速度跟踪、执行器功率和身体稳定性方面与反向传播训练的PPO基线相当，同时相比时间反向传播（BPTT）将GPU内存效率提升了4.3倍。
SARL: Label-Free Reinforcement Learning by Rewarding Reasoning Topology
Authors: Yifan Wang, Bolian Li, David Cho, Ruqi Zhang, Fanping Sui, Ananth Grama
First: 2026-03-30T02:54:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T14:55:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning is critical to improving large reasoning models, but its success relies heavily on verifiable rewards (RLVR), making it hard to use in open-ended domains where correctness is ambiguous and cannot be verified. Moreover, reasoning trajectories remain largely unconstrained, and optimizing solely toward the final answer can favor early exploitation over generalization. In this work, we ask whether general reasoning ability can be improved by teaching models how to think (the structure of reasoning) rather than what to produce (the outcome of reasoning), and we extend traditional RLVR to open-ended settings. We introduce Structure-Aware Reinforcement Learning (SARL), a label-free framework that constructs per-response reasoning maps from intermediate thinking steps and rewards their reasoning topology. SARL shifts supervision from destination to path, encouraging reasoning trajectories that are both locally coherent and globally efficient. On verifiable math tasks, SARL outperforms prior label-free RL baselines and even exceeds RL methods with ground truth supervision, with average gains of +9.1% under PPO and +11.6% under GRPO across four math benchmarks, with particularly large improvements on AIME25 (+35.5% with PPO and +44.7% with GRPO). On non-verifiable open-ended tasks, SARL achieves average gains of +34.6% under PPO and +30.4% under GRPO on WildBench across five task categories, outperforming prior label-free RL methods and DPO, which relies on additional preference labels. Beyond strong performance, SARL exhibits substantially lower KL divergence and higher policy entropy, indicating more stable and exploratory training dynamics. Code and data are available at \href{https://github.com/cacayaya/SARL}{Code Link}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SARL：通过奖励推理拓扑实现无标签强化学习
强化学习对于改进大型推理模型至关重要，但其成功高度依赖于可验证奖励（RLVR），这使得在正确性模糊且无法验证的开放领域难以应用。此外，推理轨迹在很大程度上仍不受约束，仅针对最终答案进行优化可能偏向于早期利用而非泛化。在这项工作中，我们探究是否可以通过教导模型如何思考（推理的结构）而非产生什么（推理的结果）来提升通用推理能力，并将传统RLVR扩展到开放场景。我们提出结构感知强化学习（SARL），这是一种无标签框架，从中间推理步骤构建每个响应的推理图，并奖励其推理拓扑。SARL将监督从目标转向路径，鼓励既局部连贯又全局高效的推理轨迹。在可验证的数学任务上，SARL优于先前的无标签强化学习基线，甚至超过使用真实标签监督的强化学习方法，在四个数学基准测试中，PPO下平均提升+9.1%，GRPO下平均提升+11.6%，其中在AIME25上提升尤为显著（PPO下+35.5%，GRPO下+44.7%）。在不可验证的开放任务上，SARL在WildBench的五个任务类别中，PPO下平均提升+34.6%，GRPO下平均提升+30.4%，优于先前的无标签强化学习方法和依赖额外偏好标签的DPO。除了强大的性能外，SARL还表现出显著更低的KL散度和更高的策略熵，表明训练动态更稳定且更具探索性。代码和数据可在\href{https://github.com/cacayaya/SARL}{代码链接}获取。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) in open-ended domains where correctness is ambiguous. The authors propose Structure-Aware Reinforcement Learning (SARL), a label-free framework that constructs reasoning maps from intermediate thinking steps and rewards the topology of reasoning rather than the final answer. On verifiable math tasks, SARL outperforms prior label-free RL baselines and even exceeds RL methods with ground truth supervision, achieving average gains of +9.1% under PPO and +11.6% under GRPO across four benchmarks, with notable improvements on AIME25 (+35.5% with PPO and +44.7% with GRPO). On non-verifiable open-ended tasks, SARL achieves average gains of +34.6% under PPO and +30.4% under GRPO on WildBench, outperforming prior label-free RL methods and DPO, while also exhibiting lower KL divergence and higher policy entropy for more stable training.
本文针对在开放领域中使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）因正确性模糊而受限的问题，提出了一种无标签框架——结构感知强化学习（SARL）。该方法从中间推理步骤构建推理图，并奖励推理拓扑结构而非最终答案。在可验证的数学任务上，SARL优于先前的无标签强化学习基线，甚至超过了使用真实标签监督的强化学习方法，在四个数学基准上平均提升+9.1%（PPO）和+11.6%（GRPO），其中在AIME25上提升显著（PPO +35.5%，GRPO +44.7%）。在不可验证的开放任务上，SARL在WildBench的五个任务类别中平均提升+34.6%（PPO）和+30.4%（GRPO），优于先前的无标签强化学习方法和依赖偏好标签的DPO，同时展现出更低的KL散度和更高的策略熵，表明训练过程更稳定且更具探索性。
MAGIC: Multi-Step Advantage-Gated Causal Influence for Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Haohan Yu, Jinmiao Cong, Shengzhi Wang, Lu Wang, Chanjuan Liu
First: 2026-05-03T10:05:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T14:23:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A key challenge in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) lies in designing learning signals that effectively promote coordination among agents. Designing such signals requires estimating how one agent's current action affects its teammates over future interaction steps. To address this, we introduce Multi-step Advantage-Gated Interventional Causal MARL (MAGIC), a framework that estimates multi-step action effects between agents and selectively converts them into intrinsic rewards. MAGIC uses counterfactual action interventions to compare teammate futures under factual and counterfactual branches, and introduces a gate based on advantage to direct exploration toward beneficial behaviors aligned with the task goal. Experiments on Multi-Agent Particle Environments (MPE) and StarCraft micromanagement benchmarks (SMAC and SMACv2) show that MAGIC consistently outperforms leading prior methods, with average relative final performance improvements of 26.9% and 10.1%, respectively.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MAGIC：多步优势门控因果影响用于多智能体强化学习
多智能体强化学习（MARL）中的一个关键挑战在于设计能有效促进智能体间协作的学习信号。设计此类信号需要估计一个智能体的当前动作如何影响其队友在未来的交互步骤。为此，我们提出了多步优势门控干预因果MARL（MAGIC）框架，该框架估计智能体间的多步动作效应，并选择性地将其转化为内在奖励。MAGIC利用反事实动作干预，比较事实分支与反事实分支下队友的未来状态，并引入基于优势的门控机制，引导探索朝向有益于任务目标的行为。在多智能体粒子环境（MPE）及星际争霸微观管理基准（SMAC和SMACv2）上的实验表明，MAGIC持续优于领先的现有方法，平均最终相对性能提升分别达到26.9%和10.1%。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes MAGIC, a multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that addresses the challenge of designing coordination-promoting learning signals by estimating multi-step causal effects between agents' actions. The method uses counterfactual action interventions to compare teammates' future trajectories under factual and counterfactual scenarios, and employs an advantage-based gate to convert beneficial causal influences into intrinsic rewards for guided exploration. Experiments on MPE, SMAC, and SMACv2 benchmarks show that MAGIC consistently outperforms prior methods, achieving average relative final performance improvements of 26.9% and 10.1% respectively.
该论文提出MAGIC框架，针对多智能体强化学习中如何设计促进协作的学习信号这一挑战，通过估计智能体间动作的多步因果效应来解决。该方法利用反事实动作干预，比较事实与反事实分支下队友的未来轨迹，并引入基于优势的门控机制，将有价值的因果影响转化为内在奖励以引导探索。在MPE、SMAC和SMACv2基准上的实验表明，MAGIC持续优于现有方法，平均相对最终性能分别提升26.9%和10.1%。
Improving Text-to-Image Generation with Intrinsic Self-Confidence Rewards
Authors: Seungwook Kim, Minsu Cho
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-01T04:39:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T14:01:21+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, accepted to CVPR 2026. Project page https://wookiekim.github.io/SOLACE/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Text-to-image generation powers content creation across design, media, and data augmentation. Post-training of text-to-image generative models is a promising path to improve human preference alignment, factuality, and aesthetics. We introduce SOLACE (Self-Originating LAtent Confidence Estimation), a post-training framework that replaces external reward supervision with an internal self-confidence signal: we re-noise the model's own outputs and measure how accurately it recovers the injected noise, treating low reconstruction error as high self-confidence. SOLACE converts this intrinsic signal into scalar rewards for reinforcement learning, requiring no external reward models, annotators, or preference data. By reinforcing high-confidence generations, SOLACE delivers consistent gains in compositional generation, text rendering, and text-image alignment. Integrating SOLACE with external rewards yields complementary improvements while alleviating reward hacking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于内在自置信度奖励的文本到图像生成改进
文本到图像生成驱动着设计、媒体和数据增强等领域的内容创作。对文本到图像生成模型进行后训练是提升其与人类偏好对齐、事实性和美学效果的一条有前景的路径。我们提出了SOLACE（自生潜在置信度估计），这是一种后训练框架，用内部自置信度信号替代外部奖励监督：我们对模型自身的输出重新添加噪声，并测量其恢复注入噪声的准确度，将低重建误差视为高自置信度。SOLACE将此内在信号转化为用于强化学习的标量奖励，无需外部奖励模型、标注者或偏好数据。通过强化高置信度生成，SOLACE在组合生成、文本渲染和文本-图像对齐方面持续带来提升。将SOLACE与外部奖励结合可产生互补性改进，同时缓解奖励破解问题。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SOLACE, a post-training framework for text-to-image generation that replaces external reward supervision with an intrinsic self-confidence signal. The method works by re-noising the model's own outputs and measuring how accurately it recovers the injected noise, using low reconstruction error as an indicator of high self-confidence, which is then converted into scalar rewards for reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that SOLACE delivers consistent gains in compositional generation, text rendering, and text-image alignment, and when integrated with external rewards, it yields complementary improvements while alleviating reward hacking.
该论文提出了SOLACE，一种用于文本到图像生成的后训练框架，用内在的自信心信号替代外部奖励监督。该方法通过对模型自身输出重新加噪并测量其恢复注入噪声的准确度，将低重建误差视为高自信心的指标，进而转化为强化学习的标量奖励。实验结果表明，SOLACE在组合生成、文本渲染和图文对齐方面持续提升性能，并且与外部奖励结合时能产生互补改进，同时缓解奖励破解问题。
LILO: Bayesian Optimization with Natural Language Feedback
Authors: Katarzyna Kobalczyk, Zhiyuan Jerry Lin, Benjamin Letham, Zhuokai Zhao, Maximilian Balandat, Eytan Bakshy
Venue: Proceedings of the 43rd International Conference on Machine Learning, Seoul, South Korea. PMLR 306, 2026
First: 2025-10-20T15:41:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T13:10:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many real-world optimization problems are guided by complex, subjective preferences that are difficult to express as explicit closed-form objectives. In response, we introduce Language-in-the-Loop Optimization (LILO), a Bayesian optimization (BO) framework that employs a large language model (LLM) to translate free-form natural language feedback and prior knowledge from a decision maker into structured preference signals, going beyond the restrictive scalar or pairwise feedback formats typically assumed in preferential BO. The LLM-derived preferences are integrated by a Gaussian process proxy model, enabling principled acquisition-driven exploration with calibrated uncertainty. By placing the LLM in a supporting role rather than as the optimizer itself, LILO preserves the sample efficiency and stability of BO while providing a flexible and expressive feedback interface. Across synthetic and real-world benchmarks, LILO consistently outperforms both conventional preference-based BO methods and LLM-only optimizers, with particularly strong gains in feedback-limited regimes.
Summary / 总结
LILO addresses the challenge of optimizing under complex, subjective preferences that are hard to formalize. It introduces a Bayesian optimization framework that uses a large language model to convert free-form natural language feedback and prior knowledge from a decision maker into structured preference signals, which are then integrated by a Gaussian process proxy model for principled exploration. Experiments on synthetic and real-world benchmarks show that LILO consistently outperforms both conventional preference-based BO methods and LLM-only optimizers, especially when feedback is limited.
LILO旨在解决在复杂、主观且难以形式化的偏好下进行优化的难题。它提出了一种贝叶斯优化框架，利用大语言模型将决策者的自由形式自然语言反馈和先验知识转化为结构化偏好信号，并通过高斯过程代理模型进行整合以实现有原则的探索。在合成和真实世界基准上的实验表明，LILO在性能上始终优于传统的基于偏好的贝叶斯优化方法和仅使用大语言模型的优化器，尤其在反馈受限的情况下表现更为突出。
Simulus: Combining Improvements in Sample-Efficient World Model Agents
Authors: Lior Cohen, Kaixin Wang, Bingyi Kang, Uri Gadot, Shie Mannor
First: 2025-02-17T08:06:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T12:01:50+00:00
Comments: Revised version: updated title, abstract, and framing to better reflect our contributions and situate the work within the literature
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
World models (WMs) represent the frontier of sample-efficient reinforcement learning, but their complexity leaves many promising improvements unrealized due to the significant expertise and effort required to identify and integrate them. Inspired by Rainbow, which showed that individually known improvements to DQN complement each other and can be effectively combined, we take on this challenge and ask whether the same principle applies to world model agents. We introduce Simulus, a modular token-based WM agent that integrates: (1) a flexible tokenization framework supporting arbitrary combinations of observation and action modalities; (2) intrinsic motivation for epistemic uncertainty reduction; (3) prioritized world model replay; and (4) regression-as-classification for reward and return prediction. Simulus achieves state-of-the-art sample efficiency for planning-free WMs across three diverse benchmarks: visual Atari 100K, continuous-control DMC Proprioception 500K, and symbolic Craftax-1M. Notably, intrinsic motivation proves beneficial even under the tight interaction budgets of sample-efficient RL, despite the risk of wasting scarce interactions on task-irrelevant experience. Ablation studies reveal that each component contributes individually, and their combination yields synergistic gains. Our code and model weights are publicly available at https://github.com/leor-c/Simulus.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Simulus：结合样本高效世界模型智能体的改进
世界模型代表了样本高效强化学习的前沿，但其复杂性导致许多有前景的改进因识别和整合所需的大量专业知识和努力而未能实现。受Rainbow的启发——该研究表明DQN的已知改进相互补充并可有效结合——我们迎接这一挑战，探究相同原则是否适用于世界模型智能体。我们提出Simulus，一种模块化的基于令牌的世界模型智能体，整合了：(1) 支持任意观察和动作模态组合的灵活令牌化框架；(2) 用于减少认知不确定性的内在动机；(3) 优先世界模型回放；(4) 将回归视为分类用于奖励和回报预测。Simulus在三个不同基准上实现了无规划世界模型的最优样本效率：视觉Atari 100K、连续控制DMC本体感觉500K和符号Craftax-1M。值得注意的是，即使在样本高效强化学习的严格交互预算下，内在动机也被证明是有益的，尽管存在将稀缺交互浪费在任务无关经验上的风险。消融研究表明每个组件单独贡献，且其组合产生协同增益。我们的代码和模型权重公开于https://github.com/leor-c/Simulus。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Simulus, a modular token-based world model agent designed to improve sample efficiency in reinforcement learning by combining multiple complementary techniques. The method integrates a flexible tokenization framework for diverse observation and action modalities, intrinsic motivation for epistemic uncertainty reduction, prioritized world model replay, and regression-as-classification for reward and return prediction. Experimental results demonstrate that Simulus achieves state-of-the-art sample efficiency for planning-free world models across three benchmarks: visual Atari 100K, continuous-control DMC Proprioception 500K, and symbolic Craftax-1M, with ablation studies confirming that each component contributes individually and their combination yields synergistic gains.
该论文提出了Simulus，一种模块化的基于令牌的世界模型智能体，旨在通过结合多种互补技术提高强化学习中的样本效率。该方法集成了灵活的令牌化框架以处理多种观察和动作模态、用于认知不确定性减少的内在动机、优先化的世界模型回放以及将回归视为分类的奖励和回报预测。实验结果表明，Simulus在三个不同基准测试（视觉Atari 100K、连续控制DMC Proprioception 500K和符号Craftax-1M）中，对于无规划的世界模型实现了最先进的样本效率，消融研究证实每个组件单独贡献，且它们的组合产生了协同增益。
From Passive Reuse to Active Reasoning: Grounding Large Language Models for Neuro-Symbolic Experience Replay
Authors: Yanan Xiao, Yixiang Tang, Zechen Feng, Lu Jiang, Minghao Yin, Pengyang Wang
First: 2026-05-10T08:41:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T08:41:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While experience replay is essential for data efficiency in reinforcement learning (RL), standard methods treat the replay buffer as a passive memory system, prioritizing samples based on numerical prediction errors rather than their semantic significance. This approach stands in contrast to human learning, which accelerates mastery by actively abstracting fragmented experiences into behavioral rules. To bridge this gap, we propose Neuro-Symbolic Experience Replay (NSER), a framework that transforms experience replay from a passive sample reuse mechanism into an active engine for knowledge construction. Specifically, NSER addresses the incompatibility between linguistic reasoning and numerical optimization through a novel neuro-symbolic grounding pipeline. It leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) in a zero-shot manner to induce candidate behavioral rules from accumulated trajectories, grounds these insights into differentiable first-order logic representations, and utilizes the resulting symbolic structures to dynamically reweight the replay distribution. By allowing abstract knowledge to directly shape policy optimization, NSER achieves consistent superior sample efficiency and convergence speed across reactive, rule-based, and procedural benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从被动回放到主动推理：面向神经符号经验回放的大语言模型接地
尽管经验回放对于强化学习中的数据效率至关重要，但标准方法将回放缓冲区视为被动记忆系统，基于数值预测误差而非语义重要性对样本进行优先级排序。这种方法与人类学习形成对比，后者通过主动将碎片化经验抽象为行为规则来加速掌握。为弥合这一差距，我们提出神经符号经验回放（NSER），该框架将经验回放从被动样本重用机制转变为主动知识构建引擎。具体而言，NSER通过新颖的神经符号接地流程解决语言推理与数值优化之间的不兼容性。它利用大语言模型以零样本方式从累积轨迹中归纳候选行为规则，将这些见解接地为可微的一阶逻辑表示，并利用所得符号结构动态重新加权回放分布。通过允许抽象知识直接塑造策略优化，NSER在反应式、基于规则和程序化基准测试中均实现了一致的卓越样本效率和收敛速度。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Neuro-Symbolic Experience Replay (NSER), motivated by the limitation of standard experience replay in reinforcement learning, which treats the replay buffer as a passive memory system relying on numerical prediction errors rather than semantic significance. NSER transforms this into an active reasoning process by using Large Language Models in a zero-shot manner to induce candidate behavioral rules from trajectories, grounding these rules into differentiable first-order logic representations to dynamically reweight the replay distribution. Experimental results across reactive, rule-based, and procedural benchmarks demonstrate that NSER achieves consistent superior sample efficiency and convergence speed compared to baseline methods.
该论文提出了神经符号经验回放（NSER），其动机在于标准经验回放方法将回放缓冲区视为被动记忆系统，仅依赖数值预测误差而非语义重要性，这与人类通过主动抽象经验形成行为规则的学习方式相悖。NSER通过利用大型语言模型以零样本方式从累积轨迹中归纳候选行为规则，将这些规则转化为可微的一阶逻辑表示，并利用所得符号结构动态重新加权回放分布，从而将经验回放从被动样本复用转变为主动知识构建。在反应式、基于规则和程序化基准上的实验结果表明，NSER在样本效率和收敛速度上持续优于基线方法。
Multi-scale Predictive Representations for Goal-conditioned Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Valliappan Chidambaram Adaikkappan, David Meger, Sai Rajeswar, Pietro Mazzaglia
First: 2026-05-10T06:27:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T06:27:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates robust representation learning in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL). Particularly in sparse reward scenarios, learning representations that align state and goal latents is a challenge that frequently culminates in representation divergence where the encoder drifts toward a low-dimensional, goal-agnostic subspace that destabilizes policy learning. We address this issue by showing that an agent must acquire a fundamental understanding of its environment across multiple scales, from local physical dynamics to long-horizon goal-directed structure. Building on this insight, we propose Ms.PR, a framework that leverages multi-scale predictive supervision to enforce goal-directed alignment within the latent space. We demonstrate that Ms.PR leads to improved representation quality and strong performance on both vision and state-based tasks. Furthermore, we show that our approach is exceptionally resilient under realistic, challenging data regimes, maintaining state-of-the-art performance across a wide variety of tasks, trajectory stitching scenarios, and extreme noise conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向目标条件强化学习的多尺度预测表征
本文研究了离线目标条件强化学习中的鲁棒表征学习问题。特别是在稀疏奖励场景下，学习对齐状态与目标潜在表征的挑战常导致表征发散，即编码器漂移至低维、与目标无关的子空间，从而破坏策略学习的稳定性。我们通过论证智能体必须跨多个尺度（从局部物理动力学到长程目标导向结构）获取对环境的根本理解来解决该问题。基于此洞察，我们提出Ms.PR框架，利用多尺度预测监督强制潜在空间中的目标导向对齐。实验表明，Ms.PR在视觉与状态类任务中均能提升表征质量并取得优异性能。此外，我们的方法在现实挑战性数据场景下展现出卓越鲁棒性，在多种任务、轨迹拼接场景及极端噪声条件下均保持最先进性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses representation divergence in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL), particularly under sparse rewards, where the encoder collapses into a goal-agnostic subspace and destabilizes policy learning. The authors propose Ms.PR, a framework that enforces goal-directed latent alignment through multi-scale predictive supervision, capturing both local dynamics and long-horizon structure. Experiments show that Ms.PR improves representation quality and achieves state-of-the-art performance on vision and state-based tasks, with strong resilience to realistic challenges like trajectory stitching and extreme noise.
本文针对离线目标条件强化学习中的表示发散问题，尤其是在稀疏奖励场景下编码器退化为与目标无关的低维子空间导致策略学习不稳定。作者提出Ms.PR框架，通过多尺度预测监督强制潜在空间中的目标对齐，同时捕捉局部物理动态和长期目标导向结构。实验表明，Ms.PR提升了表示质量，在视觉和状态任务上达到最先进性能，并在轨迹拼接和极端噪声等现实挑战下表现出极强的鲁棒性。
Skill-R1: Agent Skill Evolution via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yash Vishe, Rohan Surana, Xunyi Jiang, Zihan Huang, Xintong Li, Nikki Lijing Kuang, Tong Yu, Ryan A. Rossi, Jingbo Shang, Julian McAuley, Junda Wu
First: 2026-05-10T06:19:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T06:19:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic large language models often rely on skills, reusable natural language procedures that guide planning, action, and tool use. In practice, skills are typically improved through prompt engineering or by aligning the task LLM itself, which is costly, model-specific, and often infeasible for closed-source models. Skill optimization is not a one-step problem but a recurrent process with two coupled levels of credit assignment: a useful skill must improve rollout quality under current conditioning, while a useful revision must turn observed outcomes into a better skill for the next round. We propose Skill-R1, a reinforcement learning framework for instance-level recurrent skill optimization from verifiable rewards. Rather than updating the task LLM, Skill-R1 trains a lightweight skill generator that conditions on the task context, prior rollouts, and their verified outcomes to produce skills that steer a frozen task LLM. This preserves black-box compatibility with both open- and closed-source models while making adaptation substantially cheaper than model-level updates. Skill-R1 proceeds over multiple generations: at each step, the current skill induces rollouts whose verified outcomes are fed back to produce the next revision. To optimize this recurrent process, we introduce a bi-level group-relative policy optimization objective combining intra-generation and inter-generation advantages. The intra-generation term compares rollouts under shared skill conditioning, while the inter-generation term rewards revisions that improve behavior across successive generations. Together, these provide a principled objective for directional skill evolution rather than one-shot self-refinement. Empirically, Skill-R1 achieves consistent gains over no-skill baselines and standard GRPO across benchmarks with verifiable rewards, with particularly strong improvements on complex, multi-step tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Skill-R1：通过强化学习实现智能体技能进化
智能体大语言模型通常依赖技能——可重用的自然语言程序，用于指导规划、行动和工具使用。实践中，技能通常通过提示工程或调整任务LLM本身来改进，这成本高昂、具有模型特异性，且对闭源模型往往不可行。技能优化并非一步到位的问题，而是一个循环过程，包含两个耦合的信用分配层级：有用的技能必须改善当前条件下的轨迹质量，而有用的修订必须将观察到的结果转化为下一轮更好的技能。我们提出Skill-R1，一种基于可验证奖励的实例级循环技能优化强化学习框架。Skill-R1不更新任务LLM，而是训练一个轻量级技能生成器，该生成器根据任务上下文、先前轨迹及其验证结果来生成技能，从而引导冻结的任务LLM。这保持了与开源和闭源模型的黑盒兼容性，同时使适应成本远低于模型级更新。Skill-R1在多个世代中推进：每一步，当前技能诱导出轨迹，其验证结果被反馈以产生下一次修订。为优化这一循环过程，我们引入了一种双层组相对策略优化目标，结合了代内和代间优势。代内项比较共享技能条件下的轨迹，而代间项奖励那些在连续世代中改善行为的修订。两者共同为定向技能进化（而非一次性自我改进）提供了原则性目标。实验表明，在具有可验证奖励的基准测试中，Skill-R1相较于无技能基线和标准GRPO取得了持续改进，在复杂多步任务上尤其显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Skill-R1, a reinforcement learning framework designed to optimize agent skills—reusable natural language procedures—for large language models without updating the task LLM itself. The motivation stems from the limitations of existing skill improvement methods, which are costly, model-specific, or infeasible for closed-source models, and the challenge of recurrent skill optimization requiring two-level credit assignment. Skill-R1 trains a lightweight skill generator that conditions on task context, prior rollouts, and verified outcomes to produce skills for a frozen task LLM, using a novel bi-level group-relative policy optimization objective with intra-generation and inter-generation advantages. Experimental results show that Skill-R1 achieves consistent improvements over no-skill baselines and standard GRPO across benchmarks with verifiable rewards, particularly excelling on complex, multi-step tasks.
本文提出了Skill-R1，一种基于强化学习的框架，用于优化大型语言模型的智能体技能（可重用的自然语言程序），而无需更新任务LLM本身。其动机源于现有技能改进方法的局限性，这些方法成本高、依赖特定模型或无法用于闭源模型，且技能优化需要两级信用分配的循环过程。Skill-R1训练一个轻量级技能生成器，根据任务上下文、先前执行结果和验证结果生成技能，以指导冻结的任务LLM，并采用一种新颖的双层组相对策略优化目标，结合代内和代间优势。实验结果表明，Skill-R1在具有可验证奖励的基准测试中，相较于无技能基线和标准GRPO取得了持续改进，尤其在复杂多步任务上表现突出。
Functional Graphs for Predicting and Explaining Goal Failure in Sparse Goal-Conditioned RL
Authors: Shalley Dash
First: 2026-05-10T05:16:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T05:16:51+00:00
Comments: 9 pages main, 21 pages appendx, 2 figures in main. 8 figures in appendix, Submitted to a conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse goal-conditioned reinforcement learning can produce policies whose failures are hidden by aggregate success rates. We analyze trained goal-conditioned value policies through the deterministic functional graphs induced by greedy evaluation: for each goal, every state maps to a single successor, decomposing behavior into attractors and basins. This reveals a local-to-global structure in learned policies. We define local goal support (LGS), a one-step statistic measuring the fraction of valid neighboring states whose greedy successor is the goal. In deterministic sparse GridWorlds, zero LGS exactly precludes goal entry from non-goal starts. Empirically, weak LGS is a strong diagnostic of goal-level failure across update rules, curricula, larger grids, and bottleneck geometries: the fixed rule LGS <= 0.5 identifies low-success goals with precision 0.921, recall 0.929, and F1 0.925 in the main 8x8 TD setting, with similar performance across variants. However, local support is not sufficient for global success: some supported goals still fail because distant states are captured by competing attractors or fragmented basin structure. We therefore introduce a compact post-hoc taxonomy of policy-induced graphs -- goal-dominant, competitor-dominated, partial/contested, and fragmented -- to characterize residual failure modes beyond local support. These results show that sparse GCRL failures can be understood as structured policy-induced dynamics, and that local one-step policy structure provides a cheap post-training diagnostic for goal-level failure.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of diagnosing goal-level failures in sparse goal-conditioned reinforcement learning, where aggregate success metrics can obscure policy weaknesses. The authors propose analyzing trained policies through deterministic functional graphs induced by greedy evaluation, which decompose behavior into attractors and basins, and introduce a local goal support (LGS) statistic measuring the fraction of valid neighboring states whose greedy successor is the goal. In deterministic sparse GridWorlds, zero LGS precludes goal entry from non-goal starts, and empirically, a fixed LGS threshold of 0.5 identifies low-success goals with high precision (0.921), recall (0.929), and F1 (0.925) in the main 8x8 TD setting, with consistent performance across variants. However, local support alone is insufficient for global success, as some supported goals fail due to competing attractors or fragmented basin structures, leading to a post-hoc taxonomy of policy-induced graphs—goal-dominant, competitor-dominated, partial/contested, and fragmented—to characterize residual failure modes.
该论文针对稀疏目标条件强化学习中目标级失败诊断的挑战，提出通过贪婪评估诱导的确定性函数图分析训练策略，将行为分解为吸引子和盆地，并定义局部目标支持（LGS）统计量，衡量相邻状态中贪婪后继为目标的有效状态比例。在确定性稀疏网格世界中，零LGS完全阻止非目标起点进入目标，实验表明，在8x8 TD设置中，固定LGS阈值0.5识别低成功目标的精确率为0.921，召回率为0.929，F1分数为0.925，且在不同变体中表现一致。然而，局部支持不足以确保全局成功，部分支持的目标因竞争吸引子或碎片化盆地结构而失败，因此论文提出策略诱导图的后验分类——目标主导型、竞争者主导型、部分/争议型和碎片化型——以表征局部支持之外的残余失败模式。
Reinforcement Learning Measurement Model
Authors: Wenqian Xu, Feng Ji
First: 2026-05-10T04:02:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T04:02:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interactive assessments generate sequential process data that are not well handled by conventional item response models. Existing MDP-based measurement approaches, such as the Markov decision process measurement model (MDP-MM, LaMar, 2018), link action choices to state-action values, but their reliance on person-specific tabular value functions makes them difficult to scale beyond small, fully enumerated tasks. We propose the Reinforcement Learning Measurement Model (RLMM), a measurement framework that decouples person-level choice sensitivity from task-level value representation through a shared parametric action-value function, making estimation more computationally efficient for larger process-data settings. The model combines a Boltzmann choice rule with normalized advantages, a soft Bellman consistency penalty, and a block-coordinate MAP procedure for joint estimation, while also yielding step-level influence diagnostics for identifying behaviorally critical decisions. In peg-solitaire simulations, the RLMM achieved higher estimation accuracy and substantially lower runtime than the original MDP-MM, with advantages increasing as task complexity grew. In AQUALAB gameplay logs, the estimated person parameter was positively associated with cumulative reward, task completion, and behavioral efficiency. These results show that the RLMM extends decision-process-based psychometric models to larger and more behaviorally realistic environments while preserving an interpretable latent trait tied to decision making steps.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习测量模型
交互式评估生成的序列过程数据难以被传统项目反应模型有效处理。现有基于马尔可夫决策过程的测量方法（如马尔可夫决策过程测量模型，MDP-MM，LaMar, 2018）将动作选择与状态-动作值关联，但其依赖个体特定的表格化值函数，导致难以扩展到完全枚举的小型任务之外。我们提出强化学习测量模型（RLMM），该测量框架通过共享参数化动作值函数将个体层面的选择敏感性与任务层面的值表征解耦，从而在更大规模的过程数据场景中实现更高效的计算估计。该模型结合玻尔兹曼选择规则与归一化优势、软贝尔曼一致性惩罚以及用于联合估计的块坐标最大后验（MAP）程序，同时生成步骤级影响诊断以识别行为关键决策。在孔明棋模拟中，RLMM相比原始MDP-MM实现了更高的估计精度和显著更低的运行时间，且优势随任务复杂度增加而扩大。在AQUALAB游戏日志中，估计的个体参数与累积奖励、任务完成度及行为效率呈正相关。这些结果表明，RLMM将基于决策过程的心理测量模型扩展到更大且更具行为真实性的环境，同时保留了与决策步骤相关的可解释潜在特质。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces the Reinforcement Learning Measurement Model (RLMM) to address the limitations of existing Markov decision process-based measurement models, which struggle to scale due to their reliance on person-specific tabular value functions. The RLMM decouples person-level choice sensitivity from task-level value representation using a shared parametric action-value function, combined with a Boltzmann choice rule, normalized advantages, a soft Bellman consistency penalty, and a block-coordinate MAP estimation procedure. In peg-solitaire simulations, the RLMM achieved higher estimation accuracy and substantially lower runtime than the original MDP-MM, with advantages increasing as task complexity grew. In AQUALAB gameplay logs, the estimated person parameter was positively associated with cumulative reward, task completion, and behavioral efficiency, demonstrating the model's ability to extend decision-process-based psychometric models to larger and more behaviorally realistic environments.
该论文提出了强化学习测量模型（RLMM），以解决现有基于马尔可夫决策过程的测量模型因依赖个体特定表格化价值函数而难以扩展的问题。RLMM通过共享参数化动作价值函数将个体层面的选择敏感性与任务层面的价值表示解耦，并结合玻尔兹曼选择规则、归一化优势、软贝尔曼一致性惩罚以及块坐标最大后验估计程序。在独立钻石棋模拟中，RLMM相比原始MDP-MM实现了更高的估计精度和显著更低的运行时间，且优势随任务复杂度增加而扩大。在AQUALAB游戏日志中，估计的个体参数与累积奖励、任务完成度和行为效率呈正相关，表明该模型能将基于决策过程的心理测量模型扩展到更大、更行为真实的环境。
